Page 6

Page 7

Current Commentary

The Initiation and Convening of the Silver Conference

I have often said that the importance of the Silver Conference lies in whether there can be sincere cooperation and genuine willingness to sacrifice, not in who initiates it or which country the location belongs to. This conference is a global issue, not a problem of any one country. However, a conference cannot be held without a location and someone to initiate and convene it. However, looking at the attitudes of various countries now, they all express a strong desire to support it, but none are willing to initiate and convene it. The United States and Britain have already expressed this, and Japan has also unofficially decided not to initiate this conference. According to a Reuters report, Japan is unwilling to initiate because the success of the conference is still doubtful. The United States, Britain, and Japan are the countries most closely related to the silver issue, and yet none are willing to initiate it. This is already strange. Apart from the United States, Britain, and Japan, China is the country that originally proposed it, and it would be acceptable to initiate and convene it. However, according to a Washington report, the US government says that China's convening of this conference cannot move people, and a Tokyo report says that the Japanese side also

believes that it is not very appropriate for China, as a silver standard country, to convene it. If China is not suitable to convene it, then which other country is more suitable? The interests of silver-using countries and gold-using countries in the silver conference issue are very different. The purpose of gold-using countries is to save their declining trade with China, and trade with China differs in concept according to the size of power. Therefore, the success of this issue is truly in doubt. However, because it is doubtful and they are unwilling to initiate it, their hearts are already insincere. The so-called support is mostly a matter of form. Alas.

Domestic Important Telegrams

Saving the World: The sources of all disputes and chaos in the world, and the suffering of the people, are nothing more than three: first, ethnic disputes; second, political disputes; and third, economic disputes. If these three kinds of disputes do not cease, humanity will never enjoy the happiness of peace and harmony. The only way to eliminate these three kinds of disputes is through the Three Principles of the People. When nationalism is realized, all ethnic groups will be equal, and each will be able to pursue its legitimate progress and development, and ethnic disputes will cease. When democracy is realized, there will be a division of powers and functions, the government will be competent, and the people will have rights. There will never be concern about the government's autocracy and oppression, and political disputes will cease. When the people's livelihood is realized, men and women, young and old, will enjoy the happiness of food, clothing, housing, and transportation. The classes of rich and poor will disappear, and economic disputes will have no use. Its profundity and breadth are beyond the reach of narrow-minded communism, nationalism, and the like. All ethnic groups need the Three Principles of the People, and the Chinese nation especially needs them at this critical juncture of survival. Moreover, Mr. Sun Yat-sen not only had profound and broad principles, but also clearly showed us practical and feasible methods and steps in his nation-building strategies and nation-building program. This conference hereby represents all the people in respectfully accepting Mr. Sun Yat-sen's entire legacy and doing our best to promote its realization. All of our fellow countrymen should know that the Three Principles of the People are the only compass for saving the country. All nationals have the responsibility to realize the Three Principles of the People and should sincerely and earnestly strive to implement them in order to create a solemn and splendid Republic of China. This is the first message from this conference to all of our fellow countrymen.

(II) The Chinese people have been bound by a autocratic political system for thousands of years, without the opportunity to participate in politics, and their political capabilities are very weak. After the revolution, they cannot jump directly from military rule to constitutional government, and must go through a stage of political tutelage. During this period, the rule of law should be practiced, the people should be guided, and local self-government should be implemented so that the people can receive full political training in order to participate in national affairs. Mr. Sun Yat-sen spoke of this in detail in his legacy. Now that the National Government has put down the rebellion, the country has indeed moved away from military rule and entered the period of political tutelage. This conference hereby follows Mr. Sun Yat-sen's legacy and formulates the Provisional Constitution of the Republic of China for the Period of Political Tutelage, and submits it to the National Government for promulgation and implementation. This provisional constitution has eight chapters and eighty-nine articles, which contain essential regulations regarding the rights and obligations of the people, the people's livelihood, national education, the powers of the central and local governments, and the organization of the government. What is particularly important is the chapter on the Outline of Political Tutelage, which is used to determine the political program for the period of political tutelage, as well as the powers and responsibilities of the Chinese Kuomintang and the National Government during the period of political tutelage, so as to promote constitutional government. This is something that no national constitution has, and is unique to the Provisional Constitution of the Republic of China for the Period of Political Tutelage. All of our fellow countrymen should know that the provisional constitution is the fundamental law during the period of political tutelage. Whether the country can enter constitutional government depends entirely on whether the provisional constitution during the period of political tutelage can be promoted without obstruction. Therefore, all of our fellow countrymen should believe in and abide by the provisional constitution, and swear to protect it with all our strength. Anyone who dares to destroy the provisional constitution will be regarded as a public enemy, so that the provisional constitution can maintain its dignity, political tutelage can be completed, and constitutional government can be realized. This is the second message from this conference to all of our fellow countrymen.

(III) Unequal treaties are the most important tool for political and economic aggression against our country by various countries. Examining the circumstances under which these treaties were concluded at the time, there were only two types: either the defeated Qing Dynasty swallowed its anger and was willing to form an alliance under the city walls, and the other party, with the remaining power of victory, could take whatever it wanted, and any harsh conditions could be established; or the powers took advantage of the ignorance of the Qing government, its lack of understanding of the general trend of the world, and the principles of international diplomacy, and used diplomatic means to trick it into concluding treaties that harmed its independence without realizing it. At that time, most people's national consciousness had not yet awakened, and their national concept was very weak. They did not know how to resist these unequal treaties that bound our freedom and endangered our survival. The National Revolution led by Mr. Sun Yat-sen sought freedom and equality for China, and unequal treaties were the biggest obstacle to the success of the revolution. Therefore, he called on the people to abolish unequal treaties, which were both stipulated in the political program and repeatedly emphasized in his will. The people, after being awakened by the enlightened, also realized this. Since the Republic of China, the movement to abolish treaties has spread throughout the country. However, when the warlord government occupied Beiping, it considered it a good idea to attach itself to imperialism, and this movement never succeeded. Now, fortunately, the warlords have been eliminated and the country is unified. Under the National Government, the abolition of treaties is imminent. This conference represents the people and dares not shirk this responsibility. Therefore, it unanimously decided: 1. The Chinese people do not recognize any unequal treaties previously imposed on China by various countries. 2. The National Government should follow the Premier's legacy and realize the complete equality and freedom of the Republic of China in the international arena in the shortest possible time, and solemnly declare to the world that our people should know that these unequal treaties not only endanger the survival of our country and nation, but also violate justice and fairness and are a stain on human civilization. In the past, when people's intelligence was not developed, their existence could be tolerated. After the European War, new trends surged and the principle of national self-determination shone like the sun and stars. This kind of restraint imposed by one nation on another is difficult to tolerate again. Countries such as Turkey have already broken free from their shackles and restored their freedom. How can the Chinese nation be the only one to lag behind? All of our fellow countrymen should make their final determination and greatest efforts to support the National Government in completing this mission. This is the third message from this conference to all of our fellow countrymen.

(IV) The obstacles to the National Revolution in the past were imperialism abroad and warlords who were attached to imperialism at home. Now that the warlords who were attached to imperialism have been gradually eliminated, the Red bandits who are nurtured by Red imperialism have risen up again. Their crimes are a hundred times worse than those of the warlords. Their ferocity and brutality are beyond description. For several years, various places have been ravaged by them, especially Jiangxi, Hunan, and Hubei. Wherever they go, they kill and burn, and stop at nothing. Good people are massacred, and no one, male or female, young or old, is spared. They even make sons kill their fathers and brothers kill their brothers for pleasure. The cruelty of their torture makes the victims wish for a quick death but they cannot get it, those who see it are heartbroken, and those who hear about it are saddened. What Huang Chao and Li Chuang and others could not do, they do it without regret. In addition to the massacre, they also carry out destruction. Government offices and civilian houses are all burned to the ground. Food, livestock, clothing, utensils, and all means of subsistence are gone. The people in the bandit areas, even if they are lucky enough to escape, have no way to survive. Countless people wander, starve, and die. According to statistics, the area that has been afflicted by bandits has reached more than 300 counties, and the loss of life and property is incalculable. If they succeed, it will not only mean the destruction of the country, but also the extinction of the race. Thinking of this makes us shudder. The National Government has made the determination to fight against the Red bandits, and large armies are gathering in Jiangxi and Hubei provinces, striving to eradicate their roots and destroy their nests in the shortest possible time. However, the tangible Red bandits can be suppressed by military force, but the intangible Red bandits cannot be eliminated without the unanimous determination of the people of the whole country. All of our fellow countrymen must know that the scourge of the Red bandits is a hundred-generation disaster for our nation. Fathers should teach their sons, and brothers should encourage their brothers. Everyone should take it as their responsibility to eliminate the Red bandits and earnestly implement the resolutions of this conference on eliminating the Red bandits. Only then can the Red disaster be eliminated and the foundation of the country be consolidated. This is the fourth message from this conference to all of our fellow countrymen.

(V) In the past few years, the central government has been forced to use force to fight against new and old warlords, and the people have been displaced and sacrificed greatly. Only today have we achieved peace and unity. While we celebrate the success of peace and unity, on the one hand, we should express our highest respect to the officers and soldiers who sacrificed their lives for their country, and on the other hand, we cannot but attribute it to the ability of the National Government to inherit the legacy and lead effectively, without avoiding difficulties and hardships, in order to achieve this result. Moreover, the National Government has not only had great success in military affairs, but also has made considerable achievements in politics, diplomacy, education, and construction. Although the extent of the achievements may not be as expected by everyone, the spirit of the leaders in charge, who are courageous, progressive, diligent, and tireless, has long been understood by the world. Moreover, the National Government has been based in Nanjing for only four years, and has unified the country for less than three years. In addition, it has been busy with military affairs and has not had a moment to rest. Yet it has still been able to achieve so much, which makes us deeply gratified. This conference hereby represents the people of the whole country in expressing its extreme trust in the National Government. Now that the military affairs have come to an end and political tutelage has just begun, this conference deeply hopes that the National Government will continue its spirit of sacrifice and struggle, lead the people, complete the work of political tutelage, and complete the great cause of nation-building. It is especially hoped that all of our fellow countrymen, having known the preciousness of peace and unity, will support peace and unity, and support the National Government that has created this situation of peace and unity. Those who dare to violate the orders of the National Government and destroy peace and unity should be eliminated by the power of the whole country, so that the work of political tutelage can be completed as soon as possible, constitutional government can be realized as soon as possible, the Chinese nation can stand independently in the world, and the people can enjoy true happiness. This is the fifth message from this conference to all of our fellow countrymen.

(VI) Today, the livelihood of the Chinese people is extremely impoverished. To solve the problem of the people's livelihood, industrial construction is the first priority. Industrial construction has myriad aspects. This conference hereby formulates special provisions in the provisional constitution based on Mr. Sun Yat-sen's industrial plan, listing its important principles. It is hoped that the government and the people will have the same aspirations, and during the period of political tutelage, they will devote all their efforts to the people's construction cause, revitalize the rural areas, exploit mineral resources, dredge important rivers, and develop basic industries. All important matters such as navigation, aviation, port construction, road construction, immigration, and land reclamation should be pursued with practical and feasible plans to achieve success day by day and month by month. The government should support the development of the people's economic undertakings, and the people should assist in the success of the national economic construction, so that education and training can be combined, conservation can be properly carried out, people can be used to the best of their abilities, land can be used to the fullest extent, goods can be used to the fullest extent, and goods can flow smoothly, so as to reverse the past poverty and decline of our nation and open up a new path for the development and prosperity of the national economy. This is the sixth message from this conference to all of our fellow countrymen.

Moreover, in the past two hundred years, the speed of scientific progress of the Western nations has set a new record in history. This is indeed a major advance in human civilization. However, Western culture, with aggression as its center, has become a hegemonic culture. With the progress of science, it is like a tiger with wings, and the flames of aggression are becoming more and more intense. As a result, the crisis of war is becoming more and more urgent, and the techniques of human self-destruction are becoming more and more novel. Those who use force to oppress each other will inevitably perish together. This can be asserted. Although science is prosperous, mankind has not been able to fully benefit from it, but has become a tool for warmongers. This is not the fault of science itself, but the fault of hegemonic culture. To seek this remedy, we must follow the path shown by Mr. Sun Yat-sen, restore our country's inherent culture of benevolence, and supplement it with Western science to create a world of the Three Principles of the People. This will not only enable our weak nation to revive, but also prevent the crisis of human self-destruction. I deeply hope that all of our fellow countrymen, from now on, will be of one mind and one heart, follow Mr. Sun Yat-sen's legacy, encourage ourselves with the heart of establishing ourselves and others, and take on the responsibility of saving the country and the world, so that the great harmony of the world will be transformed from an ideal into a reality. It is not difficult. All of my fellow countrymen, let us encourage each other. This is the declaration. (Sixteenth Special Telegram)

Accepting the Premier's Legacy Combined With the General Assembly Declaration

(Nanjing) The Drafting Committee for the Declaration on Accepting the Premier's Entire Legacy reported that, having been assigned the task of drafting a declaration on accepting the Premier's legacy, it convened a meeting at 3:00 PM on the 15th of this month in the Second Review Room on the second floor of the assembly hall. The meeting was attended by Wang Shufang, Zhang Fengjiu, Hu Boyue, Ye Chucang, Di Ying, Wang Shijie, and Shao Lizi, seven people in total. All agreed that accepting the Premier's teachings was one of the important resolutions of the conference. This important expression of meaning must not be missing in the general declaration of the conference. In order to avoid duplication and to make the general declaration of the conference more substantial, and to make the expression of the general assembly's acceptance of the Premier's entire legacy particularly solemn, it is proposed to incorporate the section on the nation's respectful acceptance of the Premier's legacy into the general declaration of the assembly. Whether this is appropriate is respectfully requested for review. Respectfully submitted to the Presidium, convener Ye Chucang.

Message to the Guangdong Soldiers

(Nanjing) The National Assembly's telegram to all the soldiers in Guangdong: To all the soldiers in Guangdong, after Chief Commander Chen's Jiang telegram was sent, this conference formally sent a telegram of warning with a unanimous resolution. Chief Commander Chen, as a member of the party and heavily entrusted with military affairs, rashly made inappropriate remarks, revealing signs of change. The right and wrong of obedience and disobedience have already been made clear, and the success or failure can be easily predicted. Even with the errors in Chief Commander Chen's words and actions, we still could not help but express our regret and hope that he would repent. How much more so should the officers and soldiers, who have always adhered to the Premier's principles and participated in revolutionary wars, encourage each other with a word at this critical juncture of fortune and misfortune, success and failure? Peace and unity are what the Premier taught throughout his life and have long been unanimously supported by this National Assembly. The unity of all the people is clear for all to see. Anyone who violates the trend and attempts to rebel will be destroyed immediately, without the need for divination. In the past, warlords who played with soldiers and harmed the country, when popular opinion was not fully expressed, still met their doom one after another. How much more so today, when the country has a central government, the people have a voice, and party discipline and national law are clear throughout the universe? How can dew exist under the scorching sun? Moreover, revolutionary force should be united with the people, and revolutionary force is the force of the people. This is what the Premier always expected of revolutionary soldiers. Revolutionary soldiers are only driven by principles and cannot be tools for individuals. Revolutionary soldiers are happy to die for the country and are unwilling to sacrifice themselves for individuals. Therefore, their careers and achievements spread throughout the universe and are passed down endlessly. Non-revolutionary soldiers can be lured with benefits and threatened with power. In the past, warlords harmed the country by using their personal desires to drive their officers and soldiers, and the officers and soldiers, because they had not been influenced by principles, blindly followed and willingly suffered from robbery, which was of no benefit to the country and ultimately harmed themselves. Nothing is more painful than this. The honor and disgrace of revolutionary soldiers and non-revolutionary soldiers are clearly distinguished. It can be seen that true revolutionary troops will never be driven by traitors. The officers and soldiers in Guangdong have long resided in the source of the revolution. They have been deeply influenced by the Premier's legacy and national discipline. They already understand this. Chief Commander Chen is a government official and should obey. Now he suddenly makes inappropriate remarks. If he does not realize his own errors, then he is not upright himself, how can he issue orders that can be carried out? This conference deeply knows that the soldiers stationed in Guangdong have a revolutionary history and have long made extraordinary achievements. At this time of obedience and disobedience, success and failure, they naturally have a way to be loyal to the party and the country. Looking forward to the future, we are filled with concern. We express these thoughts earnestly, and hope that you will consider them carefully. The National Assembly. (Sixteenth Special Telegram)

Letter to the People of Guangdong

(Nanjing) The National Assembly's letter to the people of Guangdong: To all the people of Guangdong, since the four supervisory committee members Deng, Lin, Xiao, and Gu released their 30th telegram, followed by Chief Commander Chen's Jiang telegram, picking up on superficial words and confusing the public, the whole country was shocked and public opinion was confused. In recent days, Japanese newspapers have reported that the headquarters of the Eighth Route Army is actively preparing for military action in order to threaten the central government. In the past, before warlords played with soldiers and started wars, scholars would flatter them and first use telegrams to support them, and the content was nothing more than the beginning of conflict. This time, the incident in Guangdong province unfortunately followed the same pattern as the military actions of previous warlords. The content of the telegram from the four supervisory committee members claimed to be an impeachment of the government. It is not our intention to interfere with the supervisory committee members exercising their supervisory powers over the party's government. However, since the Central Supervisory Committee has recognized the impeachment by the four supervisory committee members as untrue and refused to accept it, Deng, Lin, Xiao, and Gu, as supervisory committee members, should obey the decision of the Supervisory Committee, and people outside the Supervisory Committee should not have any opinions on this matter. The Central Supervisory Committee's reply to Deng, Lin, and others has just been disclosed, and Chief Commander Chen suddenly issued a Jiang telegram, picking up on the untrue impeachment of Deng, Lin, and others to endanger the world's view. On what basis and from what standpoint did Chief Commander Chen make these irresponsible remarks? We, representatives of the people of the whole country, attending the National Assembly, are accepting the Premier's legacy and discussing the provisional constitution for the period of political tutelage, and are working with the people of the whole country to promote the realization of the Three Principles of the People and to build a solid foundation for the nation for ten thousand years. After discussing the provisional constitution, we have also sent a telegram to the whole country to support peace and unity and to warn Chief Commander Chen. Guangdong is a part of the territory of the Republic of China and the interests of the Cantonese compatriots of the Republic of China are vested in it. It cannot be allowed to be occupied by a few soldiers, nor can a few soldiers be allowed to gamble with it. If, unfortunately, someone uses this as a basis to make trouble, not only will the peace of the whole country be destroyed, but the local security will also be shaken. Moreover, the Red atmosphere on the border of Hunan and Jiangxi has not subsided. If they come howling, they will immediately ravage the area. Those who are afflicted by the Red bandits will be able to profit from the situation. How can all of our Cantonese compatriots bear to be fish in the pond again? With this critical juncture of interests, we are already aware of the situation. Guangdong is the source of the revolution, and all the Cantonese compatriots are deeply immersed in the Premier's legacy. The great cause of loving peace and unity has long been known to every household. The superstition of regional prejudice must be clearly distinguished and carefully considered. The limbs of the body are originally one, and the country and the local are originally related to each other. At this time of peace and danger, governance and chaos, we all have the heart of Ning Ren to stop the matter. This conference hereby expresses its infinite hope to our beloved Cantonese compatriots. We deeply believe that our beloved Cantonese compatriots have a closer view and must be true to the truth. For the actions of a few unscrupulous soldiers in destroying peace and disrupting discipline, there is no need for this conference to urge them, and they will be able to rise up in justice, protect the central government, and use their steadfast spirit to quell the chaos with a wave of their hand. Looking at the sea and the sky from afar, we cannot express our concern. (Sixteenth Special Telegram)

Chiang Kai-shek and Zhang Xueliang's Banquet for Representatives

Chiang Kai-shek's Speech at the Banquet

(Nanjing) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and Zhang Xueliang hosted a banquet for the representatives of the National Assembly at the Lichi Society at 6:00 PM on the 16th. Central Committee members Yu Youren, Dai Chuanxian, He Yingqin, Wang Zhengting, as well as Panchen Lama, Ma Fuxiang, and Chen Shaokuan, etc., entered the banquet at 6:30 PM. First, Li Songquan performed magic, and then Mrs. Diao Minqian sang a solo. Halfway through the banquet, Chiang Kai-shek gave a speech, saying that the National Assembly was the first in the history of the Republic of China. Now that the representatives have completed their responsibilities, they can not only comfort the people of the country, but also comfort the Premier's spirit in heaven. Before the meeting, the representatives had accepted the Premier's legacy and had also sworn an oath in front of the Premier's tomb. Although many of the representatives are not members of the party, they can be said to be followers of the Premier after these two expressions. It is hoped that you will still join our party so that we can work together. Furthermore, the Kuomintang is a combination of the people of the whole country, not a special political party. Now that the representatives elected by the people of the whole country have accepted the Premier's legacy, it can be said that the people of the whole country have joined. After you join the Kuomintang, you must know that it is not just about hanging a false name. It is about abiding by the party's discipline, following the Premier's legacy, realizing the Three Principles of the People, and completing the National Revolution. After the National Assembly closes tomorrow, if you can meet with us more before leaving Nanjing and tell us about the situation in various places, we will be very grateful. Now, with the utmost sincerity, I respectfully wish you good health with a glass of water. Then, Yang Daguang, a representative from Liaoning, gave a speech. Finally, the revolutionary epic film "The Revolution in Marseilles" was shown, and the banquet ended at 11:00 PM. (Sixteenth Special Telegram)

Contents of Important Proposals

Proposal to Return National Private Enterprises

(Nanjing) National Assembly representatives Sun Shihua and 51 others proposed the proposal to return national private enterprises, with the following reasons: The property of the people shall not be sealed or confiscated unless in accordance with the law. This is the established practice of a country ruled by law, and it is also stated in the draft provisional constitution. Moreover, our country's industry and commerce are still in their infancy and should be protected and encouraged in order to develop the national economy. However, in recent years, the government has often confiscated private enterprises, such as Zhenhua Power Plant in Qishuyan, Jiangsu, Pulin Electric Light Company in Henan, and Dayou Electric Plant in Changxing Coal Mine, Zhejiang. People are anxious and industry and commerce are hesitant. The sixth item in the political renovation plan of the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee last year states that enterprises with monopolistic characteristics and enterprises that cannot be operated by private individuals shall be operated by state capital. This is indeed clearly stipulated in our party's political program. However, today, when the economy has not yet developed and construction is just beginning, state-owned enterprises have no concrete scale, and private industries should be encouraged and given appropriate protection. However, the government often misunderstands the essence of the political program, does not distinguish between the importance of relationships, and disregards the feelings of the people, and often considers it a good idea to take back private enterprises. What is particularly criticized by the general public is the recovery of small private electrical businesses and the confiscation of private mines that have just begun to sprout. This has made the people fearful and suspicious that the government is using its power to compete with the people for profits. For industrial and commercial enterprises, they have all warned each other not to invest. This has driven capital out of the industry, made the national economy increasingly depressed, and helped international aggression. It is unclear about the essentials of politics and is almost cumbersome. The above proposal was passed by the Fifth General Assembly. The main text states that the scope of powers for the management and operation of state-owned enterprises should be clearly defined so that private enterprises can be protected. State-owned enterprises should be established and operated purely with state capital, and the boundaries should be clearly defined so that there is no room for misunderstanding. However, the central government's decision has been made for a long time, and the government has only returned the Pulin Electric Light Company in Henan, leaving the people still in a state of anxiety and shock, which is not the phenomenon that a country ruled by law should have. The method is to request the government to quickly return the confiscated national private enterprises, such as Zhenhua Power Plant in Qishuyan, Jiangsu, Changxing Coal Mine in Zhejiang, Dayou Electric Plant, etc., so that private property can be protected and people can be at ease. Is this appropriate? Please make a public decision at the General Assembly. (Sixteenth Special Telegram)

Please Negotiate to Abolish Harsh American Regulations

(Nanjing) National Assembly overseas Chinese representatives Huang Boyao and Zheng Zhannan proposed that the National Assembly send a letter to the National Government to negotiate with the United States that when the children of Chinese merchants enter the country, they can enjoy the freedom of merchants entering and leaving the United States as stipulated in the Sino-American Commercial Treaty after reaching adulthood. In the past, the children of our country's merchants were allowed to enter the United States with passports and permanently enjoyed the freedom of merchants entering and leaving the United States as stipulated in the Sino-American Commercial Treaty. However, since July 1, 1924, when the US government promulgated and implemented the new immigration law, it stipulates that when they reach the age of 20, the freedom of merchants entering and leaving the United States as stipulated in the Sino-American Commercial Treaty is not only completely deprived, but also after they reach adulthood, managing their father's business or operating their own business, they cannot obtain the qualifications of a merchant and enjoy the right to enter and leave the United States. The severity of the immigration law is to make our country's merchants disappear in the United States. There is nothing more unjust than this. Therefore, it is specially proposed to send a letter to the National Government to quickly negotiate with the US government to abolish this harsh regulation implemented on July 1, 1924, and restore the freedom of the children of our country's merchants to enter the country and still be able to enjoy the freedom of merchants entering and leaving the United States as stipulated in the Sino-American Commercial Treaty after reaching adulthood. Is this appropriate? Please make a public decision. (Sixteenth Special Telegram)

Page 8

Request to Enact a Stamp Tax Law

(Nanjing) Yu Xiaochuan and others propose enacting a stamp tax law. They state that stamp tax is considered a good tax in various countries, both East and West. While its collection scope is broad, the levy is minimal, and its established regulations are clear and consistent, avoiding frequent changes. Therefore, the tax law is implemented smoothly without obstruction, and the people live in peace without disturbance. In our country, since August of the 16th year of the Republic [1927], the Central Political Council deliberated and approved the "Provisional Regulations for Stamp Tax," drafted by the Ministry of Finance. In November of the same year, the Ministry of Finance announced its implementation. However, a regulation labeled as "provisional" implies that it still requires formal provisions. Yet, over three years have passed without any formal regulations drafted by the Ministry of Finance being submitted to the Central Political Council for decision on principles, or to the Legislative Yuan for content review, so that it can be formally established. During these three years, the Ministry of Finance has frequently supplemented the regulations approved by the Central Political Council, implementing these supplements through ministerial orders. It is no wonder that officials only focus on maximizing revenue, leaving merchants with nowhere to turn, and turning a good tax into a nearly evil one. They propose suggesting that the government submit the "Provisional Regulations for Stamp Tax" drafted by the Ministry of Finance in the 16th year of the Republic to the Legislative Yuan for review and enactment of a stamp tax law. Those aspects of the provisional regulations that are excessively detailed or repetitive should be deleted. For example, invoices are merely a type of notification from merchants, yet they are hastily deemed receipts. Recently, even shipping letters must be stamped, which is far-fetched and meaningless. Also, for items like pawn tickets, due to the recent soaring prices of goods, the amount pawned for a padded coat or quilt by the poor often exceeds four yuan. Since they are already pawning items due to poverty, why further burden them with stamp tax? Repetitive taxes include various license fees for tobacco and alcohol and fees for brokerage. Licenses and brokerage fees already serve as proof of tax payment. Therefore, there is a certificate because taxes are paid, and then taxes are paid because there is a certificate. As for the stipulated penalties, even minor oversights, such as a missing stamp or failure to fully stamp and seal, are punished with fines ranging from one hundred to ten yuan. Insufficient stamping is also penalized with fifty to five yuan per item. For example, a missing one-cent stamp on a shipping invoice is penalized with one hundred yuan, a tenfold increase. Or a one-cent shortfall is penalized with fifty yuan, a fivefold increase. Such penalties are rarely heard of, both domestically and internationally. Those aspects not included in the provisional regulations but expanded and added over time should be exempted. For example, tax tickets from old tax offices and customs checkpoints must all be stamped, with Jiangxi imposing the heaviest rate of three percent. Jiangsu province also imposes varying rates of two, four, and one-tenth of a cent. If the new tax is implemented in the future, there will inevitably be widespread imitation, which the people cannot bear. When the people pay taxes to the government, the government provides a proof of remittance. How can this be compared to a merchant's receipt of silver? If this example is not eliminated, even grain merchants and tenant farmers will be required to stamp. Furthermore, membership certificates for trade associations and guilds are currently being notified by various stamp tax bureaus to be stamped. It is unclear whether the regulations stipulate that personnel credentials each have special ineffectiveness. For example, a doctor's license proves medical competence, and a graduation certificate demonstrates academic progress. Trade association and guild memberships merely serve as a sign of recognition for joining the association. Forcing them to be stamped is completely unreasonable. The above are just a few prominent examples. The Ministry of Finance uses orders to supplement the law, and this is not limited to these instances. What is particularly alarming is that while the country is now unified, stamp tax tickets alone cannot be used in different counties. The restrictions are extremely strict. The tax system is flawed and urgently needs reform. It is especially necessary to request the government to instruct the Ministry of Finance to order the stamp tax bureaus to assess the prosperity of local commerce in each county and adjust the tax quotas accordingly, without setting an increase as the precondition, lest street-level sales occur, which harms the government's image, and excessive demands and harsh punishments disturb the people. Whether the implementation of a good tax stems from good legislation is appropriate for public decision.

Proposal to Abolish Coastal Export Tax

(Nanjing) Yu Xiaochuan and others propose that the coastal export tax should be abolished immediately. The export tax from one port to another is a type of domestic transit tax. In July of the 16th year of the Republic [1927], the National Government planned to eliminate it along with the likin tax. It was stipulated within the regulations for abolishing domestic border taxes that it should be implemented on September 1st of the same year. However, due to sudden military emergencies and financial difficulties, and to reclaim tariff rights, a gradual approach through negotiation was adopted, and it was not implemented as scheduled. Now that tariff autonomy has been implemented and all likin and other transit taxes have been abolished, this coastal export tax should naturally be abolished immediately. However, it has been delayed, causing deep regret among merchants and citizens. This tax is entirely domestic in nature and unrelated to national border tariffs. However, in 1860, the Qing government's treaties with England and France regarding the Tianjin Agreement and trade regulations included provisions for inland transit duties and coastal taxes. This led to the loss of domestic taxation rights to foreigners and subjected us to unilateral agreements. Foreigners wanted to protect their coastal trade and succeeded, while China believed that this would not affect regular customs revenue and could supplement financial income, but failed to recognize the loss of national sovereignty and the hindrance to industry. The imbalance and unfairness were greater than that of the likin tax. Now that the likin tax has been abolished, domestic products can flow freely, benefiting from mutual adjustment. However, goods transported from customs locations still bear this unfair transit tax. For example, silk sent from inland areas to Danyang via the post office is tax-free, but if sent to Zhenjiang, a 5% ad valorem tax is required. Silk and satin produced in Jiangsu are tax-free when sent to the inland areas via the post office, but Nanjing and Zhenjiang, being customs locations, must pay the coastal tax. Others who need to pass through customs locations due to inconvenient inland transportation do not need to pay this tax. For example, the native cloth of southern provinces in the current unified tax system must be taxed when transported to the Northeast and coarse grains transported to Fujian and Guangdong must also be taxed. Coal needed in Jiangsu is tax-free when transported by the Tianjin-Pukou Railway, but taxed if transported by ships. From a local perspective, the burden falls exclusively on places where customs are established, which seems unfair. From a broader perspective, inconvenient domestic transportation means that bulk commercial goods must be transported by ships through customs, and are all subject to this burden. This is out of step with global trends and hinders the development of national industry and business. In order to thoroughly abolish the likin tax, promote national economic development, it is appropriate to immediately abolish the coastal export tax. Whether this is appropriate is submitted for public decision.

Resolution on Suppressing Bandits

(Continued from Yesterday)

(Nanjing) Fifth, the people in the bandit suppression areas must cooperate with the county government in implementing the Baojia system, clearing the countryside, and other auxiliary bandit suppression and post-disaster affairs. Suppressing the Red bandits requires not only the national army's advance but also the people's assistance. Whether or not the assistance is effective depends entirely on whether the people themselves have a strong organization. County autonomy is a necessary organization for local people. However, in the bandit-affected areas, before county autonomy can be prepared according to law, the government must give the people of each county the strength, guarantee, and assistance to carry out the Baojia system and organize self-defense. Only in this way can the people's own strength be established, and then they can use their own strength to assist the government in suppressing the bandits. Once the organization of the Baojia and self-defense strength is established, the people should cooperate with the national army. When the national army advances to suppress the Red bandits, they should secretly investigate the bandits, report on bandit traces, manage transportation, and engage in propaganda. When clearing the countryside in their respective counties, they should investigate bandit criminals and cut off their traces, leaving no one at large. After the bandits are cleared, they should cooperate with the government to handle the recruitment of refugees, relief to the injured, restoration of order, and other post-disaster matters. The government must promote, encourage, and protect the people in carrying out these tasks, and the people must, under the government's encouragement and protection, strive to fulfill their responsibilities. Then the suppression of the Red bandits will surely achieve rapid results. Therefore, in the future, cooperation between the people and the government to eliminate the bandit scourge must take the organization of the people's own strength as the primary task. The people across the country should provide cooperation and support to the government. As for the people's hopes for the government, they can be divided into two aspects: fundamental and superficial. The cause of the Red bandits arises externally from the incitement of Red imperialism and internally from the exhaustion of the people's livelihoods, as mentioned earlier. Therefore, in suppressing the Red bandits, in terms of fundamental solutions, the government must strive for material construction to open up avenues for national livelihood and prosperity. At the same time, it must consolidate national unity and peace, and rectify the official governance and administration of the provinces to eliminate opportunities for bandits to incite chaos. Once internal governance is on the right track, the national economy and political power can be used to strengthen national defense and foster good relations with foreign countries. Not only will the Red bandits inevitably disappear due to the severance of internal and external resources, but the country can also achieve long-term stability. This fundamental solution does not require further elaboration. As for what the current congress hopes from the government, in terms of superficial solutions, it hopes that the government will enforce strict rewards and punishments for the bandit suppression army, and replenish their supplies and equipment so that bandit suppression can be more effective. Secondly, it hopes that the government will provide as much relief as possible to the disaster-stricken people in the bandit areas so that they can be properly settled, resume cultivation, and eliminate the source of incitement. The various unified measures and regulations needed for the people across the country to assist the government in suppressing the Red bandits should also be promptly planned and formulated by the government. It is deeply hoped that the entire country, from top to bottom, will, in accordance with the resolution of this case, pool their wisdom and efforts to eliminate this major disaster for the future of the Chinese nation in the shortest possible time. Once this disaster is eliminated, the country's peace and unity will be more complete, and the order and tranquility of society will be more firmly established without fear of disruption. Only then will all the constructions of the Three People's Principles proceed smoothly.

Foreign Important Telegrams

Pan-European Conference Opens

Russian Delegation Arrives in Geneva

German-Polish Dispute: Germany Wins

Guomin News Agency, Geneva, 15th – The Pan-European Conference opened today with an opening address by French Foreign Minister Briand. Briand appeared very dispirited due to the unfortunate blow of the presidential election and lacked his previous vigor. Even his opening address was unremarkable. Briand merely stated that a recent proposal to organize international agricultural loans would open a new outlet for economic pressure in Europe. However, the most important item on the agenda of this conference is Germany's proposal to examine the customs policies of various European countries in order to solve Europe's economic difficulties. At this point in Briand's speech, British Foreign Secretary Henderson suddenly stood up and said that he had a personal thought that he wished to share with the chairman. Henderson then said that he was very pleased to see Briand still in the position of chairman of the international conference today. Briand is not only the greatest politician in France, but also a great politician in the world. The representatives of all countries have always admired him and he is truly worthy of being an elder statesman in the League of Nations. Briand smiled and humbly thanked him at this point, which was Briand's first smile since arriving in Geneva. Briand concluded by saying that the work in Geneva should overshadow all minor irritations and difficulties, and that if the representatives of the countries could trust him as Mr. Henderson did, then he hoped that the representatives of the countries would cooperate with him sincerely.

Reuters, Geneva, 16th – This morning, German Foreign Minister Curtius told the committee discussing the issue of a European Federation that the division of Europe into many new countries is the main cause of economic misfortune. The way to remedy this is for the countries to conclude a customs union. French Foreign Minister Briand abruptly mentioned the German-Austrian customs union in his reply, saying, "We must avoid everything that could arouse European resistance, anxiety, and harm." Briand strongly disagreed with the view that economic misfortune was caused by customs barriers, saying that high tax rates were caused by economic misfortune, not causing economic misfortune. The committee was greatly shaken by the two foreign ministers' opinions being so strongly in conflict. Soviet Russian Foreign Affairs Commissar Litvinov paid particular attention.

Guomin News Agency, Geneva, 15th – The Russian delegation arrived here this afternoon, led by Foreign Affairs Commissar Litvinov. The Russian delegation is currently staying at the Metropole Hotel, which was originally the residence of the German and Japanese delegations. The Russian delegation has now abandoned its former residence and moved into the Metropole Hotel, so there is much speculation outside.

Guomin News Agency, Geneva, 15th – The International Court of Justice today publicly ruled on the German-Polish case regarding German schools in Poland, completely following Germany's demands. Eleven people favored Germany, and only one person favored Poland, namely the Polish representative. This matter is very important and other nationalities in Poland and elsewhere will surely welcome it, as it proves that it is not only the League of Nations that protects the rights of minorities.

Guomin News Agency, Geneva, 15th – Today, the International Secretariat announced the exchange of documents between the British, French, and German governments regarding the case of Britain and Germany previously requesting countries to publish the actual state of their armaments before the disarmament conference. Among them, the British government, in response to the German government's request, asked whether it was a countermeasure to the British government's request. The German government's reply was that the principles of the British government's request and the one put forward by the German government were the same and the trends were consistent, but the German proposal was more in line with the resolutions of the League of Nations Council, and the British proposal was not as complete as the German proposal. On the other hand, the French government expressed doubts about whether it could obtain realistic reports on armaments from the countries concerned before the opening of the International Disarmament Conference.

Guomin News Agency, Geneva, 15th – Today, British Foreign Secretary Henderson invited the foreign ministers of Germany, France, and Italy to discuss the issues in the League of Nations Council meeting, and especially had in-depth discussions on the German-Austrian tax agreement and the preparations for next year's disarmament conference.

International Silver Price Conference

The United States is Prepared to Send Representatives to Participate

Japan Has No Intention of Initiating a Convocation

Reuters, Washington, 15th – Chinese Minister to the United States, Dr. Wu, has notified Deputy Secretary of State Castle that the Chinese government is now carefully considering issuing a request to convene an international silver conference soon. Castle today officially released the first statement by the US government regarding its attitude toward the silver conference, stating that the United States is prepared to participate in the international silver conference, but the US government does not have as direct a relationship to this issue as other countries, so it is best for this conference to be convened by another country.

Reuters, Washington, 15th – The New York Times today carried a dispatch from Washington stating that the US government feels that the Chinese government's convocation of an international silver conference cannot move people. Although the US government is prepared to cooperate with China, it would rather have another government initiate this conference. If Japan is the initiator, the United States will surely give a sympathetic response. The Japanese Ambassador to the United States has notified the US government that the Japanese government is now considering the issue of issuing a request to open an international silver conference. It is reported that the government's consent to consider is the result of the investigation by the Japanese representatives of the International Chamber of Commerce.

Reuters, Tokyo, 16th – Personnel from the Ministry of Finance and important figures in business circles held a meeting today to continue discussing the issue of an international silver conference. It has been informally decided that Japan should not initiate this conference because the success or failure of this conference is extremely doubtful. The general opinion is that after the Japanese government considers this matter, it will notify the US government of its intention not to convene a silver conference.

Guomin News Agency, Tokyo, 16th – Japanese Minister of Finance Inoue discussed with important figures in the banking world today the proposal to convene an international silver conference in Tokyo. At present, the Japanese economic world believes that because the UK is selling silver from India, it does not want to convene this conference urgently. The United States is also worried that it will involve war debts and is unwilling to act as the initiator. China is a silver standard country and seems to be unsuitable in terms of location. Japan, on the other hand, is a gold standard country and does not produce silver, so it is more suitable for convening this kind of conference. Therefore, it is believed that Tokyo is a suitable location for the conference, but before convening, the procedures to be discussed in the conference should be prepared in advance, which cannot be completed in a short time. Therefore, it is advocated to first organize a committee to conduct research and then take formal action.

Reuters, Mexico City, 15th – In order to prevent fluctuations in silver coins, Mexico will import a large number of American gold coins and circulate them among the people. Today, bankers held a meeting here, and their opinions were all that the public needs gold coins, and they decided to organize a banking group to manage foreign exchange and prevent speculators from suppressing silver prices. The Ministry of Finance stated that the free exchange of cash between Mexico and other countries will be realized soon. Currently, merchants in several places are telegraphing the government to find ways to alleviate the crisis, because business has now almost completely stopped.

Reuters, Ottawa, 15th – Darling, the manager of the British Midland Bank, today proposed to the Canadian House of Commons Banking and Commerce Committee to establish a supreme bank in the British Empire to consolidate the British Empire's bimetallic monetary system. Darling said that the British Empire should be at the forefront of the world movement in order to solve international monetary issues and stabilize the price of silver against gold. This kind of supreme bank will surely establish a permanent balance in the price of gold and silver. Canadian Prime Minister Bennett has met with Darling several times, and it is likely that the issue of stabilizing the bimetallic monetary system will be raised by Canada and become one of the most important items on the agenda of the British Empire Economic Conference in August.

Irwin's Speech on India

Said Indians Cannot Be Subdued by Force

Development of Commerce Requires Political Adjustment

Reuters, London, 15th – Former Indian Governor Irwin said in a speech to the Anglo-Indian Association today that he knew that some people held the view that if the government were a strong government, the Indian turmoil would not occur and everything would pass peacefully. It should be known that this kind of view is completely wrong. Even if this kind of government can get the support of public opinion today and implement policies of a cruel nature forever, the apparent tranquility it obtains is the tranquility of tragic submission, not the peace of mutual consent. The imperial ideas of the Victorian era have now passed, and have been replaced by new ideas of harmonious imperial relations. The world has long been familiar with the new ideas in the relationship between the British Empire and overseas autonomous regions, so the development of Indian ideas is also natural and inevitable. As for the rejection of British goods, he had spoken to Gandhi about it when he left Bombay, and Gandhi had made a very real promise about this. There are three things that the British people cannot but know now: one is that the economic development of India will eventually strengthen its purchasing power in all aspects; two is that after the tense atmosphere in the political situation is cleared, the expansion of India's demand will last for a long time and cannot be supplied by India itself, and British manufacturing will have good opportunities here; and three is that commerce must be based on good intentions, and the British business community should pay attention to the political adjustment of Anglo-Indian relations, so that its commercial activities are not disturbed by political ups and downs. Irwin also said that he believed that if Gandhi came to London, he would do his best to seek a compromise.

Roman Pope Denounces Capitalism

Concentrates Economic Power

Brewing Despotic Behavior

The Only Remedy Lies in Believing in Religious Social Philosophy

Reuters, Rome, 15th – The Roman Pope's encyclical on social and labor issues has now been published, opposing selfish industrialism and communism, pointing out that these are harmful fallacies, saying that a system must be organized so that ordinary people gradually attain the appropriate comfort of the assets they are given, and various professions must cooperate faithfully to replace class struggle. It also said that the economic power of the whole world is concentrated in the hands of a few people, which brews tyrannical despotism. The only remedy is to restore the sound principles of the social philosophy of the Church and its application to labor and capital. Today, there are 80,000 men and women from 22 countries gathered in the courtyard of St. Thomas Aquinas to listen to the Pope's speech. The Pope's speech was clear and lasted for more than an hour, and he was not tired. He first spoke in Italian and then translated it into French and German.

Spanish General Election

Scheduled for Late June

More Than 100 Churches Destroyed

Guomin News Agency, Madrid, 15th – The Spanish government announced that the general election will be held on June 21 or 28, and the new parliament will be convened around July 1. There have been no more disturbances in various places today. As a result of the anti-Christian riots in recent days, a total of 105 churches and monasteries have been destroyed.

Public Telegram

Changsha telegram - To all newspaper offices, Greetings. Having read the telegrams from Minister He, Director He, Commander-in-Chief Lu, and Zhen Rithong, loving the Party and protecting the country, suppressing bandits and saving the people, the language is strict, and the righteousness is correct. The Provincial Government has deleted a telegram sent by Hunan to Commander-in-Chief Chen in Guangzhou, which read: "I have read Jiang's telegram with understanding. The Republic of China has been established for twenty years. Times are difficult and banditry is rampant. Right and wrong are commonly seen, and the advantages and disadvantages should be weighed. Wise men cannot bear the devastation of the country, and benevolent men must punish the Communist bandits. If you are indifferent to power and the strife of emotions, you should also value the unification of the country, pity the suffering of the people, be careful of the opportunity for misfortune, be alarmed by the danger of the capsizing boat, and promote the atmosphere of great creation and harmony. The future of the Party and the country is deeply dependent. I hereby inform you, please consider it thoroughly." The Hunan Provincial Government respectfully deletes it.

Important News

Yesterday the National Government Held a Military Parade

National Assembly Representatives and Foreign Envoys Attended

The Inspected Troops Were the National Government's Guard Division

The National Government, on the occasion of the imminent closing of the National Assembly, held a military parade at the airfield at 9:00 AM on the 16th. National Assembly representatives were invited to attend and observe, to showcase the nation's military strength and spirit. The weather that day was clear and sunny, with a gentle spring breeze. The attendees included all representatives, members of the Central Committee and the National Government, heads of various agencies, and approximately two thousand foreign guests, including male and female envoys from various countries stationed in Beijing. The order of events was as follows: (1) Aircraft flyover, (2) Firing of ceremonial cannons, (3) Standing at attention, (4) Playing of music, (5) Singing of the Party anthem, (6) Bowing three times to the National Party flag and the portrait of the late Premier, (7) Chairman respectfully reading the Premier's last will, (8) Military parade, (9) Speech, (10) Cheering of slogans, (11) Playing of music, (12) Photography, (13) Refreshments, (14) Conclusion of the ceremony. The details of the military parade are recorded below:

Layout of the Parade Ground: At the entrance of the parade ground, there was a decorated archway, adorned with red and green embroidered balls on both sides. In the center of the field, three decorated platforms were erected, the central one being the main platform, with viewing platforms on either side. All platforms were covered with colorful cloth. On either side of the platforms were rest rooms. On the viewing platforms, seats were arranged in three tiers, with over four hundred seats for spectators. At the top of the main platform, a broadcasting system was installed for speeches.

Page 10

Details of the Military Parade: The elite troops of the Guard Division, led by Commander Feng Yi-pei, riding a horse and carrying a saber, arrived in front of the reviewing stand and reported the number of troops and their readiness. The military parade then commenced. The Commander-in-Chief's Adjutant, Wang Shi-he, led the way with the command flag. Commander-in-Chief Chiang, riding a black horse, advanced at a measured pace, followed by Zhang Xueliang, He Yingqin, Zhu Peide, Chen Yi, Cao Haosen, He Yaozu, Zhang Zhijiang, Zhang Zhizhong, Chen Diaoyuan, and others, each carrying a flag. They circled the field once for inspection and then returned to the platform, where the march-past began. The troops were divided into several columns, starting with the infantry, followed by hand-carried machine gun teams and ammunition pack horses, totaling four regiments. Next came the field artillery, mortar teams, and part of the transportation corps. This was followed by the 1st Cavalry Regiment, and finally, twenty-four tank platoons.

Speeches by Chiang and Zhang: Commander-in-Chief Chiang's speech briefly stated: "The late Premier's last will advocated convening a National Assembly and abolishing unequal treaties. It has now been seven years since the Premier passed away. Relying on the spirits of the Premier and the martyrs in heaven, as well as the efforts of all officers, soldiers, and the people of the entire nation, we have single-mindedly engaged in military revolution to establish a foundation for peaceful unification. We must unanimously protect and preserve this foundation, which was obtained through immense sacrifice. We are greatly pleased by the attendance and observation of the representatives of the National Assembly. I hope that all our officers and soldiers will continue to work hard in accordance with the resolutions passed by the National Assembly to advance unification and construction and abolish the unequal treaties, to console the spirits of the Premier and the martyrs, and to live up to the expectations of the people of the entire nation." Then Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang spoke, briefly stating that the military force of the revolutionary army is the military force of the people. Today, the representatives of the entire people are here to observe, which means we are presenting our military force to the people, a truly gratifying moment. In China's current situation, without military force, there can be no peace, unification, or construction, and we cannot achieve the goal of abolishing unequal treaties.

Military Parade Slogans: (1) The National Revolutionary Army is the military force of the people; (2) The National Revolutionary Army is an army of wisdom, benevolence, and courage; (3) Uphold the Premier's teachings; (4) Continue the spirit of the martyrs; (5) Safeguard peaceful unification; (6) Strive to strengthen national defense; (7) Eradicate the heinous Red bandits; (8) Eliminate reactionary remnants; (9) Overthrow imperialism; (10) Abolish unequal treaties; (11) Support the National Assembly; (12) Support the National Government; (13) Long live the Three Principles of the People; (14) Long live the Chinese Nationalist Party.

The Situation in Shanxi After Shang Zhen's Trip to Peiping

All Parties Eagerly Await His Early Return

Taiyuan Correspondence: After Shang Zhen's trip to Peiping, he has not yet returned to Taiyuan, and the local military and political affairs have fallen into a state of virtual stagnation. Military salaries in various regions are still being levied locally by the counties. Although there were rumors that Song, Pang, Sun, and other units had received allocations from the Deputy Department, in reality, there has been no substantial assistance. The counties are finding it extremely difficult to raise funds, while the military levies are becoming more frequent and urgent. Representatives from various counties are currently gathered in Taiyuan, but without Shang's return, there is no solution. Regarding the provincial currency lottery, it is already overdue by several days. The provincial government has requested instructions from Shang twice, but there has been no response. As a result, the credit of the provincial currency has plummeted again. Recently, the exchange rate of the provincial currency had broken through the three-yuan mark and was showing a rising trend. However, due to the lottery not being held on schedule, rumors are rampant in society, and the value is declining daily, having fallen from two yuan eighty-nine fen. The stationed troops in various parts of southern Shanxi are currently calm, but incidents of robbery are increasing daily. All parties have high expectations for Shang's trip. The future of Shanxi's situation will depend on whether Shang can find a solution during this trip, and there is a strong hope for his early return to take charge. (12th)

The various officers and soldiers were well-trained and full of spirit, which was very gratifying to observe. It is hoped that they will continue their efforts to complete the National Revolution, uphold unification and construction, and abolish unequal treaties, to fulfill their duties as citizens."
