He Jian Reorganizes Various Armies in Western Hunan

Chen Quchan Sternly Admonished

Dai Huihuan Officially Dismissed

Changsha Correspondence: Although the military forces in Hunan are nominally under the command and deployment of He Jian, in reality, the various units in western Hunan have not strictly followed provincial orders. During He Jian's recent visit to Beijing, he reported the situation in western Hunan to Commander-in-Chief Chiang in detail and strongly requested reorganization. Chen Quchan, stationed in western Hunan, has been in charge of military and political affairs and Miao defense affairs in western Hunan since succeeding Tian Yingzhao in 1920, for more than ten years. Chen has weathered many political storms and has held sway over ten counties including Yongshun, Baojing, Longshan, Sangzhi, Fenghuang, Qianyang, Sui Ning, Huangxian, Gumashan, etc. The provincial authorities, finding it beyond their reach, have had to tolerate him. In recent years, Chen's power has grown, and he was appointed by the central government as the commander of the newly organized 34th Division and concurrently as the commander of the 1st Hunan Garrison Army, under the command of the 4th Route Army. The provincial government then considered transferring him out for reorganization to unify western Hunan. Chen did not comply and instead set up numerous checkpoints within his defense zone, levying taxes on goods in transit, protection fees, and taxes on opium seedlings. In addition to the regular troops, he also recruited bandits from western Hunan and established various security corps and Miao defense teams, using various names. Military expenses were levied locally. During He Jian's recent visit to Beijing, he reported all of Chen Quchan's activities to Commander-in-Chief Chiang. Subsequently, he received orders to reorganize Chen's forces. Yesterday, He Jian, in his capacity as the Commander-in-Chief of the 4th Route Army, sent a telegram to the province, issuing a notice stating: "Received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang stating that, after investigation, Chen Quchan, commander of the newly organized 34th Division, stationed in western Hunan, due to obstructed communication and misunderstanding of the overall situation, has sometimes misunderstood the deployments of the 4th Route Army. His units have many miscellaneous titles that do not conform to the organization. The numerous checkpoints within his defense zone are particularly inconsistent with the national goal of abolishing likin. He should be clearly admonished to rectify his conduct. In the future, the division commander must strictly follow the command and control of Commander-in-Chief He in military matters. All miscellaneous titles should be strictly abolished to unify the organization. Regarding civil administration and financial affairs within the defense zone, he must strictly follow the political orders of the Hunan Provincial Government. All illegal checkpoints must be abolished to alleviate the people's suffering. He must not be confined to a corner and develop his own style. This is of utmost importance. In addition to directly ordering Division Commander Chen, you are to comply accordingly. Respectfully, Commander-in-Chief He."

Dai Huihuan's unit was also stationed in western Hunan, serving as the Commander of Bandit Suppression in Western Hunan and concurrently as the commander of the Independent 10th Brigade, commanding two brigades and four regiments. In the winter of last year, He Jian abolished the title of the Independent 10th Brigade and transferred Dai to be a counselor of the General Headquarters. All units under his command were reorganized. Dai, however, refused to comply and incited the various units to oppose He Jian. Zhang Jinwu's regiment under Chen Quchan also rose up in response, gathering in the border areas of Yuanling, Taoyuan, and Xupu. He Jian immediately dispatched Luo Shujia of the 19th Division, leading two regiments, and also telegraphed Chen Quchan and Wang Jialie of the Guizhou Army to each send a regiment to encircle and suppress them. He also took advantage of this trip to Beijing to request Commander-in-Chief Chiang to deal with Dai. Subsequently, he received Commander-in-Chief Chiang's approval to remove Dai from his position as counselor. Therefore, He Jian also telegraphed all parties yesterday, notifying them in a document stating: "Received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang stating that, after investigation, Dai Huihuan, the former commander of the Independent 10th Brigade, has already been officially transferred to serve as a counselor of this headquarters, and his units have been separately reorganized. However, it has been repeatedly reported that Dai Huihuan dared to incite his units to rebel and falsely claim that he received orders from the Commander-in-Chief to return to his original position, etc. His disregard for law and discipline has reached an extreme. Dai Huihuan is hereby dismissed from his position as counselor and will be strictly investigated and dealt with to maintain discipline. A special telegram is sent to you, hoping that you will notify all your subordinates accordingly. Respectfully, He Jian." (May 14th)

The Encirclement of He Long's Troops Has Been Completed

Thorough Elimination is Limited to Before the 20th

Hankou Correspondence: He Long's remnant bandits, previously fleeing from the Xuejiaping and Guohaping areas, have moved to various places in the Qianxi and Jianchashi areas of Yuan'an County. After being encircled and suppressed by various armies, their strength has been reduced by two-thirds. When He first fled to that area, he originally planned to cross Nanzhang and Gucheng, pass through southern Henan, and flee into Anhui to join forces with the bandit Kuang Jixun. However, Fan Shisheng's division and Wang Guangzong's brigade were deployed tightly, making it impossible to succeed. He then turned south again, attempting to secretly cross the Yangtze River via Xingshan and enter the areas of Wuhe and Yangping via Zigui, but they were also occupied by Guo Xun's brigade, and the front line connected with Wang's brigade stationed in Malingping, making it even more difficult to break through. They are currently still maneuvering on the border between Yuan'an and Nanzhang, waiting for an opportunity to move. On the government side, they are advancing from four sides. The southeast is being handled by a part of Xu Yuanquan's division, which has advanced to Yanchi and Gaoqiao. The due north is being handled by Li Zhuzhong's brigade under Fan Shisheng, which has advanced to Xiaojiayan and Leijiapo. The northwest is being handled by Zhao Guanying's division and Wang Guangzong's brigade. Zhao's division has advanced to Baokang, and Wang's brigade has advanced to Malingping. On the southwest side, it is being handled by the three regiments of Guo Xun's brigade, which have also advanced to Shuiban, northeast of Yangping. The encirclement has been completed. After receiving reports from various parties, the Wuhan Headquarters specifically ordered Xu Yuanquan, Fan Shisheng, and Zhao Guanying's three divisions, and Guo Xun and Wang Guangzong's two brigades on the 15th to continue their efforts to suppress the bandits and to completely eliminate the remaining bandits before the 20th. After receiving the orders, Xu and others immediately moved towards the bandit lairs. Guo has already made contact with the bandit forces and is coordinating with friendly forces for a second general attack, which should not be difficult to annihilate within the deadline. (May 15th)

The Storm Over the Issuance of Treasury Bonds in Fujian Province

Merchant Guilds Failed to Comply with the Order to Pay the Full Amount

The Public Security Bureau Detained Representatives

Various Groups Telegraphed Rebuttals to Fang Shengtao

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Fujian Provincial Security Department, in order to incorporate local armies into the provincial defense army, the provincial police, and the security team, needed a large amount of funds. Therefore, the provincial government issued 500,000 yuan in treasury bonds to provide funding. Of this, 320,000 yuan was allocated to the Fuzhou merchant guilds and 180,000 yuan to the Xiamen merchant guilds. In Xiamen, the head of the Xiamen branch treasury, Zheng Yinglin, contacted the General Chamber of Commerce. In Fuzhou, the Director of the Department of Finance, He Gonggan, recently hosted a banquet to invite the leaders of various guilds to discuss the loan subscription method, but all the guilds declined for various reasons, resulting in no results. The provincial government then ordered the Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Guo Yongrong, to send police on the 9th to summon representatives of various guilds to the General Chamber of Commerce to discuss the matter, setting a deadline for paying 200,000 yuan by the 10th and the remaining 200,000 yuan by the 15th. The representatives, finding the deadline too tight and the amount too large, were unable to comply. On the evening of the 9th, they held an emergency meeting at the General Chamber of Commerce. The Department of Finance specially dispatched Commissioner Wu Changcheng, leading a team of security police, to monitor the proceedings. After discussions until dawn, the guilds were only able to raise 50,000 yuan. They reported this to Guo Yongrong by telephone. Guo was extremely dissatisfied and sent a bus to the General Chamber of Commerce, detaining all twenty-four representatives and taking them to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for custody. When the guilds heard that the representatives had been detained, they held an emergency meeting on the morning of the 10th to discuss countermeasures. Guo Yongrong, hearing the news, sent more police to order the selection of two responsible persons to go to the bureau for consultation. At that time, there were fifty-two directors of various guilds present, who were willing to go together, but the police officer, finding the number too large, was unable to accommodate them and left. On the afternoon of the same day, led by the silk and cloth guild, they telegraphed the central government, the National Government, the Fujian delegation to the National Assembly, and the Fujian associations in Beijing and Shanghai, complaining about the military and police authorities forcing loans and arbitrarily detaining merchants, requesting rescue and upholding justice. However, Fang Shengtao, the Acting Chairman of the Provincial Government and concurrently the Director of the Security Department, discovered that the telegram was drafted by Chen Guang, a lawyer and legal advisor to the silk and cloth guild. On the afternoon of the 11th, he sent special agents to Chen's residence in Huangxiang Alley and took Chen to the Security Department for detention. The Lawyers Association, hearing the news, was greatly angered. On the morning of the 12th, they held a general meeting and elected the President, Wei Yifeng, and Councillor Zheng Yikang, to go to the Security Department to express their concern for Chen Guang, but they were refused a meeting. Wei and others had no choice but to return to the association and report to the members. After a general discussion, they decided to resolve the matter through legal means. The methods were as follows: 1. File a lawsuit against Fang Shengtao with the local court prosecutor's office for illegal abuse of power. 2. File a complaint with the National Government's Control Yuan against Fang for dereliction of duty and request punishment. 3. Until the case is resolved, all lawyers will suspend court appearances. The situation is currently very tense, but the police officers from the Department of Finance and the Public Security Bureau are still waiting at the General Chamber of Commerce for the payment, while some wealthy merchants, such as Luo Mianhou, Zeng Shanke, Huang Zhanhong, and You Qingkui, fearing involvement, have separately subscribed and paid. Therefore, the various merchant guilds are very dissatisfied with this. (May 13th)

The Water and Land Police Arrested Important Bandits: After the bandits from Lake Taihu, including Taibao Ashu, were captured and executed, the authorities spared no effort in strictly arresting their followers. Today (16th), the County Public Security Bureau received a report from Pan Yongqiang, the head of the 1st Branch Bureau of Tinglin, that they had escorted a bandit, Xu Bolang, to Songjiang, along with a confession. According to the confession, he used to be a tailor and is now the boat rocker for Taibao Ashu's second boat. When Taibao Ashu was at the height of his power, he had a total of six boats. The bandit was arrested at the Bajingyuan Tea House in Tinglin. In addition, Fan Guozhong, the captain of the 1st Team of the 1st District of the Waterborne Provincial Public Security, secretly ordered his subordinates to detect and arrest Yao Mulin (aka Yao Helin), a notorious recidivist, in the Small North Gate of the French Concession in Shanghai. He confessed to robbing in Zhangze, Hougang, Tinglin, Caojing, and other places, as well as burning houses in 1929, and recently robbing the Shen Maolin family in Tinglin of silver and clothing. Captain Fan prepared a document and handed him over to the County Government of this county, requesting that he be dealt with according to the Regulations for Clearing Villages. After County Magistrate Jin interrogated him, he immediately instructed that the bandit and the original documents be sent to the County Court Prosecutor's Office for investigation and legal action.

Suzhou

A Tragedy Occurred at a Rural Festival in Xiangcheng: In this county, every year on the 28th day of the third lunar month, the birthday of the Eastern Peak Emperor, villages and towns would hold festivals and plays. On the 15th, which happened to be the 28th day of the third lunar month, the Eastern Peak Temple in Xiangcheng Town outside Loumen held a religious festival. Villagers from Tangjiabang and Huangniliang, located one or two miles from the town, gathered to participate in the procession. Villagers from Huangniliang placed the statue of the deity on a boat and sailed to Tangjiabang, which was discovered by the villagers of Tangjiabang, who, fearing that Huangniliang would take the lead, gathered and intercepted the Huangniliang boat. At that time, the villagers of Huangniliang, outnumbered, abandoned the boat and returned to their village, where they gathered more people and returned to Tangjiabang to negotiate. The villagers of Tangjiabang, seeing the menacing approach, sent someone to the town to report to the security team and the merchant militia, saying that a large gang of bandits had arrived in the village, intending to rob them. Upon hearing the news, the security team and merchant militia members immediately rushed to Tangjiabang in different directions, preparing to arrest them. The villagers of Huangniliang explained the situation, but the villagers of Tangjiabang, seeing that the security team and militia members had arrived, beat the villagers of Huangniliang, and a large-scale armed fight broke out between the two sides. The security team and the merchant militia members opened fire to warn them and stepped forward to suppress the riot, but one bullet hit a Mr. Xi, piercing his chest. He fell to the ground and died on the spot. The shooter, realizing that he had caused trouble, threw a quick-firing pistol into the river and fled in panic. The villagers of Huangniliang chased down a suspect wearing a yellow uniform and reported to the 7th District Office. The assistant of the district, knowing that District Chief Zhou Zhaolin was in the city, hired a boat to come to the city and inform District Chief Zhou. District Chief Zhou went to the county and reported to County Magistrate Huang, requesting a review and handling of the matter. County Magistrate Huang, realizing that the incident involved a public official committing homicide, immediately ordered the Public Security Bureau to send officers to thoroughly investigate the truth and requested the County Court Prosecutor's Office to send officers to examine the deceased to provide a basis for review.

Prosecutor Appeals Murder Case: Chao Zhangshi, the daughter-in-law of Chao Zhengshi, a villager in Wanxuizhen, Changzhou, had an affair with Yang Jinde, a neighboring villager. Chao Zhengshi found out and scolded his daughter-in-law. Yang Jinde harbored deep resentment. On the evening of January 14th of last year, taking advantage of Chao Zhengshi's absence, he murdered Chao Zhengshi on the way. Later, the Public Security Bureau detained Yang Jinde and Chao Zhangshi and handed them over to the Wujin County Court. On April 6th of this year, the court sentenced Yang Jinde to fifteen years of imprisonment and found Chao Zhangshi not guilty. Prosecutor Yang, dissatisfied, appealed to the High Court. Yesterday (16th), the Wujin County Court sent police to escort them to Suzhou and send them to the High Court to await trial.

Wujiang

Improved Seeds Promise a Bountiful Harvest: The County-run Sericulture Farm in this county has been promoting improved varieties for many years and has gained the trust of silkworm farmers. As a result, many silkworm farmers are using improved varieties. This year, the County-run Sericulture Farm introduced more than 30,000 sheets of improved varieties, mostly crossbred varieties, mostly produced by the United Sericulture Improvement Association. The farm has also set up more than a dozen guidance stations in the villages, dispatching instructors to provide practical guidance, implementing joint warming and joint rearing of young silkworms. The silkworm rearing process has been quite good during the silkworm season. Currently, the early ones have already been moved to the cocooning frames, and the late ones have also completed their major sleep and are feeding. It is predicted that there will be a complete harvest.

Wuxi

Medical Negligence Case Spreads: Wang Yiren, an employee of the World Book Bureau in this county, because his wife Qi was pregnant and ill, hired the traditional Chinese medicine practitioner Wang Borong from the Chinese and Western Hospital for treatment. Unexpectedly, Wang misdiagnosed her with blood bloating and, after prescribing medication, caused her to miscarry twins. Qi's illness became more severe. Wang then hired a lawyer to write a complaint, accusing Wang Borong of medical negligence and causing death due to negligence, and filed a criminal lawsuit with the Prosecutor's Office, requesting that the Chinese and Western Hospital be sealed. The Prosecutor's Office, according to the complaint, yesterday summoned both parties to the case for interrogation. The plaintiff, Wang Yiren, arrived in court as summoned, but the defendant, Wang Borong, fearing punishment, did not appear. His wife, Wang Shen, appeared on his behalf. In the afternoon, Prosecutor Zhou opened the court for questioning. As a result, he ordered the plaintiff and defendant to be sent back and wait for Wang Borong to be summoned before further interrogation and review. After this case occurred, Mao Nansong, Wu Shangyi, and others published a statement in the newspaper, stating that the advertisement contained words such as "holding grudges and seeking disputes, attempting extortion." Wang Yiren believed that Mao and others published defamation in the newspaper and filed a self-accusation with the Criminal Court, accusing Mao and others of damaging his reputation and requesting punishment in accordance with Article 324 of the Criminal Law. It is not known how the court will handle it.

Chunhua Pawnshop Suffers Another Theft: Recently, many pawnshops in the county have been stolen from. For example, the Tongji Pawnshop in Yanqiao and the Baohe Pawnshop in Nanqiaozhen have suffered heavy losses. Yesterday, the jewelry room of the Chunhua Pawnshop on Huangnifeng outside the South Gate was also stolen. An apprentice, Liu, left without notifying anyone after closing the shop and did not return all night. When the staff in charge of the jewelry room checked the gold and silver jewelry, it was discovered that the jewelry with the number 29 was missing, worth more than 1,000 yuan, with a pawn value of several hundred yuan. The manager of the pawnshop, Wang Xiaofeng, sent a letter to Liu's guarantor, inviting him to the shop to discuss ways to maintain credit. The guarantor, realizing that the responsibility was significant, was unable to decline and agreed to compensate at the price. A Mr. Yan, who wanted to redeem a jade inlaid gold ring, was also unable to do so and finally agreed to compensate him with 86 silver dollars and stopped. It is reported that now the various sellers have all learned about the news of the theft of the jewelry room, and most of them are flocking to redeem their items, causing frequent disputes.

Military Police Intercept Suspicious Officer: Yesterday, when the express train on the Jinghu Railway arrived at the Wuxi Station, the military police stationed at the station boarded the train to inspect the passengers. Suddenly, they saw an officer leading three soldiers, who looked suspicious. They immediately went forward to check and found five pistols, one hundred bullets, and one thousand silver dollars. The passport had been altered. After the military police questioned him, his answers were vague. They were taken to the company headquarters and sent to the 4th Regiment's gate to prepare a document and escorted them to the Shanghai Songhu Garrison Headquarters for review.

Three Shops in Diaozhuang Robbed: At Diaozhuang, about five miles from Baijiaqiao outside the East Gate of Wu County, at about 1:00 AM on the 15th, more than a dozen armed bandits suddenly arrived. Danyang

A Robbery Occurred at the Huan Family Residence: At the Huan Zhaozong residence in the Huan Family Compound in the northern township, at 9:00 PM on the 12th of this month, more than twenty bandits suddenly rushed into the house and searched it extensively. Patrol Officer Arrested for Bribery and Protecting Local Merchants: Ma Jisheng, a patrol officer from the Second Public Security Substation in the South Gate, was suspected of bribery and protecting local merchants. Yesterday, after He Chengshen interrogated him, he sent Ma Jisheng to prison to await trial.

Zhenjiang

The Huaian pig levy cannot be revoked: Zhou Junsheng and Li Zhensan, representatives of pig merchants from Huaian County, previously petitioned for the revocation of the pig levy in the county, arguing that it was similar in nature to the likin tax. However, the county's Public Security Bureau secretly requested the Finance Department to collect the levy to subsidize police expenses, which has a significant impact on the pig business. They came to the province to petition both the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments for its revocation and submitted a written petition in person. Yesterday, the Civil Affairs Department issued a response, stating that although the pig levy within the county's police levy had previously been approved by the department and forwarded to the Finance Department for review and ordered to be revoked, the county magistrate subsequently submitted a report detailing the situation. The Finance Department then determined that the levy was collected by the pig trade when merchants invested in the trade, and it was a voluntary contribution from pig merchants to subsidize police expenses for protection, which differed from the nature of likin tax. Therefore, it could be approved, but no bureau should be established to collect it. The pig trade should be ordered to pay the designated amount of the levy to the county on a monthly basis according to the recognized amount, obtain stamped receipts, and follow the instructions. The submitted petition still used the argument of being ordered to abolish the levy and refused to pay, which was a misunderstanding. As for the claim that the head of the county Public Security Bureau fabricated facts, it was a question of whether the Finance Department's handling was appropriate. Since the merchants did not file an administrative appeal according to the law, the county followed the original plan and executed it, which was not inappropriate. The request should not be considered, etc.

Yangzhou

Two habitual thieves executed by firing squad: Zheng Desheng and Chen A’san, two habitual thieves from Yancheng who had previously organized crowds to rob Chen Shaoan's rice shop in Toudaoqiao, the Zhaoguan Dam tax office, the Huojiaqiao defense corps, the Datong Transportation Company, and other families, were apprehended by the county detective team and handed over to the county court. The court has now investigated the case, sentenced them to death, and submitted the sentence to the High Court for approval. The provincial government deliberated and approved the sentence. This morning (the 15th) at 10:00 AM, the county court bound them and took them to Kangshan for execution by firing squad.

The citizens are indignant. Levying of Acreage Tax Leads to Prison Sentences: Chen Fuqing, Wang Meiyu, Wang Jinxiu, Ding Ruiyan, Kong Xiangui, and others from the Dayi area in the eastern countryside, previously used the name of the township office to forcibly collect acreage tax in the form of rice and grain from various places. Dalian Creates Three National Records

Men’s 800m, 1500m… Women’s Long Jump The Dalian Chinese Youth held their 10th Track and Field Games on the 10th of this month. The results of each event were brilliant and remarkable, with many breaking previous records. In particular, Mr. Yu Xihui's time of 4 minutes and 24 seconds in the 1500 meters broke the national record of 4 minutes, 26 and 43/5 seconds. Mr. Yu's time of 2 minutes and 4.7 seconds in the 800 meters is also a national record. Ms. Hu Suzhi's long jump of 4.173 meters broke the national record of 4 meters. In terms of team results, the Electric Railway team in the adult category has consistently led the association in the past and won again this year. This is their third victory. The Middle Youth team in the youth category has won the championship for the third consecutive time. As for the women's team championship, which was newly added this year, it was won by Liu Ehuang and others from the Middle Youth team.

Jiangnan University Games Conclude Successfully

Central University — Wins Track and Field Championship

Jinan University — Wins Track Championship

Central Women — Wins Women's Championship

National New Record in Pole Vault Also Creates Five New Meet Records

The fifth Jiangnan University Games concluded yesterday. Central University won the track and field championship, Jinan University won the track championship, and Central Women won the women's track and field championship. A total of five new Jiangnan University records and one new national record were created at the meet. Yesterday was sunny and warm, the order was excellent, and the spectators were enthusiastic. The awards ceremony and closing ceremony were held at 5:00 PM.

One National Record

Five Meet Records—

Pole Vault — Breaks National Record

—Chen Ling of Central University — 3.495 Meters—

Pole Vault, High Hurdles, Discus, Javelin, 1500 Meters

—All Break Meet Records—

A total of five new records were created during the two-day meet. On the second day, Chen Ling's pole vault of 3.495 meters not only broke Tu Chuanzhen's Jiangnan University record of 3.45 meters, but also broke Xia Xiang's national record of 3.475 meters, adding much color to the meet. The five new meet records created were: (1) Ma Fengrui of China Public School in the 1500 meters, (2) Chen Ling of Central University in the high hurdles, (3) Wang Jihuai of Guanghua University in the javelin, (4) Gao Shangzhi of Central University in the discus, and (5) Chen Ling of Central University in the pole vault. Also, the open shot put was a national new record, but it was not officially contested.

Central University Track and Field King

—Chen Ling's Pole Vault Stands Out—

—Guanghua Takes Second Place—

In the men's track and field events, Central University won the championship with 20 points, becoming the track and field king. On the first day, Central University surpassed Jinan University by three points, with a score of ten to seven. Guanghua was only in third place with five points in the long jump. Yesterday, in the finals of the four events, Central University suddenly added six points in the pole vault, while Jinan University did not score. Thus, victory and defeat were decided. Furthermore, it is commendable that Chen Ling of Central University also set a new national record of 3.495 meters in this event. In the javelin and long jump, Wang Jihuai won two first places, and Guanghua jumped to second place. Although Zhao Rugong of Central University did not participate in this event, Jinan University only scored one point, and their hopes were dashed. Wen Dingxin could not equal his own Jiangnan University record in the javelin, only getting three points, allowing Central University to gain two points. These are the reasons for the victory and defeat.

Track and Field Scores for Each School

1st Central University 20 Points

2nd Guanghua University 16 Points

3rd Jinan University 14 Points

4th Jiaotong University 13 Points

5th Fudan University 8 Points

6th Daxia University 6 Points

7th China Public School 0 Points

Jinan University Track Champion

One Point More Than Central University

Thanks to the 200 Meters

Jinan University won the track championship, only one point more than Central University. There was a great deal of luck involved in this. The track events were originally a battle between Jinan and Central, and others had no chance to compete. Jinan excelled in short distances, while Central was strong in the high and intermediate hurdles. Central's performance in the middle distances was more impressive. Based on the above, Central seemed to have a greater chance of winning. Moreover, there was also the strong Fudan athlete Gu Zaiping in the short distances. However, Jinan, through arduous struggles, managed to win by a margin of one point. There were two reasons for this. In the 200-meter race, Gu Zaiping was highly favored, and it was difficult for Jinan's veterans Hao Chunde and Zhong Lianji to compete. Unexpectedly, the veterans showed their power, overwhelming the rising stars. Hao was first, Zhong was second, and Gu was third, while Jinan's Zeng Rongzhong also won fourth place. Central's entire team failed, resulting in Jinan scoring nine points, which was extremely influential in the overall situation. This was one reason. The last event of the track competition was the intermediate hurdles. At that time, Jinan had 25 points and Central had 18 points, a difference of seven points. Central had four participants, while Jinan had none. Among the four participants from Central, Chen Ling was almost certain to win first place. If the other three could secure a second-place finish, or two third and fourth place finishes, Central would surpass Jinan with 26 points. Even if they only managed to win a third-place finish, the scores would be tied at 25 points each, and Central would still win the championship due to having one more first-place finish (Jinan had two, Central had three). In other words, at that time, Jinan was helpless and could only wait for fate to decide. However, in reality, things changed. Chen Ling's first place was beyond doubt, but Guanghua's Tao Mojie and Jiaotong University's Zhang Jinrong occupied the second and third positions. Although Central tried hard, their strength was insufficient, and they were helpless. This was the second reason.

Central University Dominates Women’s Track and Field

—Except for Javelin and Shot Put—

—Every Other Event Had a First Place—

Central University won the women's track and field championship with ease, scoring 49 points to rank first. In the seven events, except for the javelin and shot put, every other event had a first place. Besides Central and Jinan universities, which enthusiastically participated in this year's women's track and field events, Guanghua and Fudan universities were hesitant and did not participate, which reduced the interest considerably, making it almost a contest between Central, Jinan, and Fudan universities. It is hoped that there will be uniform competition in the next meet.

Relay Performance

Important News

Record of the First Day of the Second Jiangsu Boy Scout Jamboree

The second Jiangsu Provincial Boy Scout Jamboree was held yesterday (the 16th) in Zhenjiang. The number of participants totaled over 3,700, a three-fold increase compared to the first one last year. It is also more than 300 more than the total number of participants from all provinces and cities in the first national general inspection.

Instructor Oath Ceremony Yesterday morning at 9 o'clock, the instructors from various counties held a joint oath ceremony. Those taking the oath included Wang Yongnian from Danyang, Fei from Songjiang, Ni Zegeng from Chongming, Wu Tiancai from Lianshui, Sun Shimei from Xiao County, Zhou Xisheng from Qidong, Zhao Ziqiao from Jiangning, Zhang Wenzhong from Luanshui, Tie Duo from Yancheng, Li Boying from Guanyun, Cun from Jurong, Zhu Wenyu from Fengxian, Zhu Chongming from Wu County, Chen Langying from Pei County, Hu Naisong from Shuyang, and Liu Ziruo from Liuhe, a total of twenty-six people. After the ceremony, the oath was read, followed by an address from the officiating officer Chen Bangcai. Finally, Zhu Chongming, representing the oath-takers, gave a reply.

Yesterday's Inspection and Exercise Yesterday afternoon at 2 o'clock, the groups from various counties participating in the provincial Boy Scout Jamboree gathered at the camp in the Provincial Stadium in Nanmen. They marched in formation to the County Stadium on Renzhang Road to practice the inspection ceremony. The military band of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau led the way. The teams were arranged in order of registration. At 2:30, they arrived at the stadium. Zhu Chongming served as the commander-in-chief, Zhang Hao and Ye Yangyuan as deputy commanders, and Gu Zuhua, Song Jingqi, and Dong Zhiyao as division commanders. The ceremony was led by Zi Huaizhong, director of the Jamboree Office. Commander-in-chief Zhu reported that there were 45 counties, 184 groups, and 4,115 participants. Then, Director Zi, along with representatives of the China Boy Scout Headquarters and the Central Training Department, Zhang Zhongren, Zhang Jiyao from the Shandong Provincial Party Department Guidance Section, Zhang Qiqing from the Nanjing Special Municipality Guidance Department, and Hu Pu'an, Director of the Provincial Department of Civil Affairs, and Zhang Zhongren, gave brief speeches. Then, the China Boy Scout song was sung, slogans were shouted, and the parade dispersed.

Yesterday Evening's Bonfire Party At 9 PM, a bonfire party was held at the camp. After the ceremony, the chairman reported on the meaning of the bonfire, and then the performances began. For a time, the fire blazed, a spectacle to behold. Finally, the chairman made some remarks, the Boy Scout song was sung, and the meeting adjourned.

Zhang Naiyan and Others' Educational Proposals for the National Assembly

Zhang Naiyan, a Zhejiang representative to the National Assembly, proposed a resolution to ensure the duties of those engaged in education in order to foster professionalism. The original text is as follows: Rationale: Education is a fundamental national plan, and the duties of those engaged in education are extremely important. However, there have been no regulations to truly protect them. Administrative offices often easily replace principals, and with each principal change, teachers and staff are also replaced, viewing the school as an official bureau, and teachers as hired hands. As a result, those who consider themselves noble often remain hidden, and those with talent often abandon their posts. On the one hand, there is a shortage of talent, and on the other hand, there is a struggle for position. The failure to see clear and significant results after running a school for more than a decade is not unrelated to this. Now, if we want to concentrate talent in education, effective protection is essential. Based on the above reasons, I propose the following measures: Measures: The Legislative Yuan should enact specific regulations to protect teachers and staff at all levels of schools. Those engaged in educational duties should, as a matter of principle, remain in their positions for a long time. Administrative offices and school principals should not advance or dismiss people based on personal preferences.

Another proposal states: Implement a direct minor tax dedicated to educational funding to provide universal education, assist poor and outstanding students to advance in their studies, and improve the salaries of primary school and vocational teachers.

City Elementary School Social Studies and Natural Science Exhibition

Today is the Last Day

The Social Studies and Natural Science Exhibition organized by the Municipal Education Bureau opened the day before yesterday, and this newspaper briefly reported on it. The exhibition lasted three days and was open to the public. More than 30,000 pieces of work from various schools were displayed, which were of great value for teaching. Today is the last day, and starting tomorrow, the Municipal Education Bureau will hire many experts to begin judging. Details of the exhibition are recorded below.

Types of Exhibits The exhibits include children's works, self-made new teaching tools, new teaching materials, and various reference materials, all systematically displayed for research. A total of 97 schools participated, with a total of more than 30,000 exhibits, a compilation of the achievements of various city schools in these two subjects, truly an unprecedented event.

Crowded Attendance Since its opening, in addition to students and teachers from various city schools who have been scheduled for visits for comparison and improvement, more than 10,000 guests from all walks of life have visited, praising it unanimously. The exhibition also welcomes students' families to visit, so they can understand their children's general learning in school. Admission tickets are not required for anyone visiting.

Last Day Today is the last day of the exhibition, open to the public from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM, it is said.

St. John's University Alumni Garden Party

President Bu is on Leave to Return Home

Shen Siliang is Acting President

The St. John's University Alumni Association held a garden party yesterday afternoon at 1 o'clock. The garden is located in Fanwangdu, with towering ancient trees and beautiful scenery. In addition to the clear weather after a long rain, the attendees were especially numerous. At 2:30, various games were played first on the lawn south of the garden, followed by a meeting in the social room. The chairman, Yu Hongjun, the president of the association, delivered a welcoming speech, saying, "We revisit our alma mater as if returning home after marriage, filled with joy and emotion," and so on. Next, President Bu gave a speech, saying in essence, "Today, everyone in the world is worried about the economic downturn, but this garden party at our school shows no signs of a downturn, which is very gratifying. I believe that university education is about quality, not quantity. Higher education in China has developed very rapidly in recent years, but our school has a long history and has cultivated an excellent spirit, making a significant contribution to Chinese education. I am old and will be on leave to return home this summer, and Vice President Shen will act as president. I hope the alumni will do their best to assist. Know that the difficult times for our school are far behind us, and the future should be very optimistic," and so on. Next, Mr. Wang Yunwang gave a speech, detailing his feelings about traveling to Japan, the United States, Britain, Switzerland, Belgium, and Italy. He then said that St. John's University in China, both in its history and spirit, is worthy of admiration. Today, in the diplomatic, educational, and business sectors, there are alumni of St. John's, and its influence has reached the whole country. He hoped that it would make even greater contributions in the future. Other programs included ancient music, Chinese music, Western music, and martial arts, etc. Then photos were taken and refreshments were served, and awards were given by Mrs. Yu Hongjun. The party ended in joy.

Local News

Circular Telegram from the Municipal Executive Committee

Responding to He Yingqin's Genuine Telegram

The Municipal Executive Committee, deeply indignant at the fictitious facts and slanderous accusations against comrades in the telegram of the 30th by Deng Zeru, Gu Yingfen, and others, recently received a genuine telegram from four comrades including He Yingqin, and immediately sent a telegram in response. The original text is excerpted as follows: "To Minister He, Chairman He, Chairman Lu, and Chairman He in Nanjing: We have read your genuine telegram. Unfortunately, the Party and the nation have suffered from years of war. The melons of the Yellow Terrace are plucked again and again. Fortunately, our revolutionary soldiers, under the leadership of Comrade Chiang Kai-shek, have worked together with one heart and one mind, advancing bravely, fighting for the cause, and sacrificing for the people, enabling us to eliminate warlords and unify China. Since the military settlement last year, the central government has adhered to the teachings of the Premier, devoted itself to political tutelage and construction, working hard and tirelessly. Recently, it convened the National Assembly to formulate a provisional constitution and start anew with the people. All those with blood and breath should set aside petty grievances and work together for the greater good, sacrificing private interests for public benefit, in order to deliver our compatriots from fire and water and secure the national foundation. Unexpectedly, comrades Deng Zeru, Gu Yingfen, and others, with ulterior motives, dared to issue a telegram at the beginning of the National Assembly, inciting the people's hearts, and Chen Jitang and others again took the opportunity to deploy troops, destroying peace. The news has deeply alarmed the people of Shanghai. Your telegram is full of righteousness, and your loyalty is evident. Your words are earnest and your righteousness is strict. There is no shortage of enlightened people in Guangdong and Guangxi, who will surely rise up at the sound of the wind and curb the chaos together. If Chen Jitang and others continue to be stubborn and want to lightly move troops and cause more suffering to our people, our association can only appeal to the central government to issue a clear order for suppression. The people of Shanghai are willing to be the rearguard," and so on.

The Shipping Association convened representatives of various shipping companies to the association yesterday to discuss the matter of dispatching merchant ships to Hunan. The Slaughter Tax Uproar Escalates

Butchers to Suspend Business Today

The municipal slaughter tax, since the Finance Bureau took over, has been implemented by collecting fees per head of livestock, which has aroused opposition from meat merchants, as reported in previous newspapers. It is now learned that meat merchants, unable to bear the burden and with the authorities detaining pigs, have had no choice but to suspend business, and have submitted a request to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for relief. The situation yesterday is described below.

Butchers Stop Slaughtering The slaughter tax was previously contracted by meat merchants such as Fan Chunqiu to the Jiangsu Provincial Education Funding Management Office. This time, after the municipal government took over, it implemented collection per head of livestock, which aroused opposition from meat merchants, who demanded the abolition of the slaughter tax and its replacement with a business tax, but were unsuccessful. The municipal government set the implementation date for the 16th (originally scheduled for May 1, but later extended to the 15th at the request of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to the Finance Bureau). After a meeting of the Fresh Meat Industry Association members, it was decided to stop slaughtering from the 15th. Starting today, meat merchants throughout the city will have no meat to sell and will suspend business. Pig merchants have been greatly affected, and the people also feel quite inconvenienced, it is said.

Shop Investigation The number of fresh meat businesses that have suspended operations due to the slaughter tax issue is as follows: more than 420 in Zhabei District, 13 in Jiangwan District, 17 in Wusong District, 6 in Zhenru District, 4 in Yinxiang District, 4 in Yinhang District, 7 in Beixinjing, 20 in Xinlaolonghua, 24 in Xujiahui District, 42 in Caojiadu, 13 in Gaoqiao District, 45 in Lannidu, 12 in Yangjiadu and Lujiadu, 27 in Dongjiadu, 11 in Bailianjing, 5 in Yangsi Township, 15 in Tangqiao, more than 400 in Hunan, and 120 in Tangjiawan, totaling more than 1,200. Among the fresh meat businesses in the concessions, there are more than 300 in the British Concession, such as Lu Gaojian, more than 800 in the American Concession, such as Wang Jiren, and more than 200 in the French Concession, such as Yongda. According to news from the trade association, they will rise up to help and take united action in the coming days, given their shared interests and the need to stand together, it is said.

Instructions from the Authorities The Municipal Public Security, Finance, and Health Bureaus jointly issued instructions, which stated, "In order to comply with orders, in view of the many memorial holidays in May, to prevent unscrupulous elements from inciting incidents, the Municipal Government and the Garrison Headquarters have issued announcements prohibiting strikes and market closures. It is now found that the city's fresh meat merchants are on strike to coerce the cancellation of the slaughter tax. However, the slaughter tax is a common local tax that has been in place for more than ten years. Our city has taken over in accordance with the law, and there is no reason to unreasonably obstruct it. In addition to ordering the investigation and punishment of those who obstruct and incite, we hereby order your association to earnestly inform the trade to continue business as usual, and not to be fooled by others, so as not to violate the ban. You are ordered to comply and report back for future reference."

Assistance from Various Industries More than 100 trade associations in the city, including floral, department store, seafood, grocery, refining, lace, and pawnshop industries, are indignant at the financial authorities' coercion of the meat industry to pay taxes and the detention of pigs, which has led to the suspension of business in the meat industry. Yesterday, they jointly submitted a request to the Central Party Headquarters and the National Government to immediately find a way to stop it in order to stabilize commerce. (The full text is omitted)

Yu's Intervention Mr. Yu Qiaqing, a leader in Shanghai's business community, is always very enthusiastic about protecting businessmen. In view of the fact that the meat industry consists of small businesses, he telegraphed Mayor Zhang yesterday, asking him to be considerate of the difficulties of the merchants and approve the meat industry's request, it is said.

The Meat Industry Petitions The Fresh Meat Industry Association, considering the Social Bureau to be an organization for protecting industry and commerce, sent representatives Rong Qianchu, Wang Jinwen, and others to the Social Bureau yesterday to petition. They were received by Chen Zeyi of the bureau. The representatives explained their plight and asked for help. Mr. Chen replied that it was the bureau's duty to protect industry and commerce, and that he would forward the request to the municipal government for consideration and modification. The representatives were satisfied with the result and left. The Fresh Meat Association also sent representatives Rong Qianchu, Jin Guifu, Wang Jinwen, and Huang Jikang to Nanjing to petition. They were received by Luo Jieren, a staff member of the Jiangsu Provincial Education Funding Management Office. Regarding their request, he promised to forward it to Director Niu. The representatives considered this satisfactory and returned to Shanghai the day before yesterday. They then received a batch numbered 379, which read, "We have received the presentation. The Shanghai municipal slaughter tax has been handled by the office in a letter to the municipal government. You should submit it directly for approval." This batch.

The Chamber of Commerce Submits a Document The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the National Government, the Municipal Government, and Wang Yansong, a representative to the National Assembly, stating, "On the 14th of this month, we received a letter from the City Fresh Meat Industry Association, stating that the association is now caused the city government to order the industry to buy tickets for each pig slaughtered, which has aroused unanimous opposition from the industry. The association is requested to forward this to the higher authorities and, in accordance with the one-item-one-tax system promulgated by the Central Government, cancel the slaughter tax. The association has considered this in detail. If a good solution is not actively devised, the trend among the industry will inevitably expand. Therefore, yesterday, we specially convened a general meeting of all members at the hall of your association, with more than 1,000 members attending. We have presented a request to the Municipal Training Association and the Municipal Social Bureau, as well as your association, to send representatives to attend and guide the discussion. It was unanimously decided that in addition to requesting the municipal government to change the city's pig slaughter tax to a business tax, the Municipal Health Bureau should also cancel the pre-slaughter fees charged to the industry in the concessions, as well as the post-slaughter fees charged to the industry in the interior, and the inspection fees charged by technicians dispatched from the four rural districts. Furthermore, because the municipal government recently forced the industry to buy tickets for each pig slaughtered, which caused a disturbance for a time, fortunately, Comrade Zheng Chengqing of your association and representatives of the Municipal Finance Bureau negotiated and temporarily limited this to the 15th of this month. Although peace was temporarily restored, the fundamental problem was not resolved. In the future, after the deadline, the municipal government will still want to force the industry to buy tickets and pay taxes. The general meeting also unanimously decided to request the municipal government not to force the purchase of tickets after the 15th, otherwise, it will inevitably cause a unanimous shutdown of the industry throughout the city. In addition, the municipal government's new plan is to build a new slaughterhouse near Song Park Road in Zhabei and to stop all existing commercially operated slaughterhouses. If this is implemented, the industry throughout the city will feel inconvenienced. In addition, the distance to the four rural districts is far, making travel even more inconvenient. It was also unanimously decided to request the municipal government to withdraw the order and return the operation to the industry's own regional management, improving the new slaughterhouse. The above situation has been unanimously decided at the meeting. For the sake of national taxes and the industry's future, the association should present the facts of the meeting to your association, uphold the difficulties of the industry, and request the municipal government to quickly change the city's pig slaughter tax to a business national tax. In addition, issues such as pre-slaughter and post-slaughter fees, the inspection fees of technicians from the four rural districts, and the plan for a new slaughterhouse should be canceled. The association also has a statement that the municipal government had previously limited the purchase of tickets and the collection of taxes to the 15th of this month. However, after the 15th, we still ask the municipal government not to force the collection of taxes. Before the slaughter tax is changed to a business tax, the industry will still pay according to the original tax amount to show consideration. This matter concerns national taxes and the industry's future, and is extremely urgent, awaiting your orders." It has been found that this slaughter tax has been changed from being contracted by contractors to being collected by the Municipal Finance Bureau on a per-head basis. In fact, the taxes paid are higher than before. This matter concerns the burden of the entire meat industry and is by no means a dispute over the interests of a few contractors. As for the abolition of the contractor system, in terms of tax principles, it is naturally proper. However, the situation in this city is complex. Just in terms of fresh meat, there is the provincial slaughter tax and the municipal inspection fee. Those transported to the concessions must be collected by the Public Works Department. The division of political power has caused the meat merchants to bear triple taxes, which is a unique phenomenon in Shanghai. Since the government officials, due to the situation, have been unable to unify the taxes, the meat merchants, in order to avoid excessive burdens, request to maintain the original contract. It is inevitable. The unification of the tax system and the abolition of contractors are mutually related. It is not permissible to only consider the abolition of contractors as a proper move to reorganize the tax system, and to dismiss the meat merchants' position with one-sided beneficial matters. Taking the inspection fee of this city as an example, the annual income, based on the agreed contract amount of the previous year alone, is already more than 22,000 yuan. The municipal treasury relies on this as a tax source, which has exceeded the actual inspection cost. In the past, when municipal taxes were not abundant, although meat merchants had overlapping burdens, the power was in the hands of the officials, or it was unavoidable. Now, the business tax for various industries is about to be implemented, and the Pudong wharf donation has also been recovered for some time. The increase in the city's treasury should be more than one million. On the one hand, there are new taxes to increase revenue, and on the other hand, there should be a reorganization of the tax system, so that the people can be taxed without excessive burdens. Before the meat merchants' overlapping burdens are eliminated and the business tax is not changed, they request that the slaughter tax still be paid according to the original tax amount. According to the above situation, there is indeed reason. It is appropriate to telegraph your office to review and approve, and to order the municipal government to approve as requested, which is in the public interest.

Second Day of Health Week Activities

Yesterday was the second day of the 7th Shanghai Municipal Health Week. The details of various activities are recorded as follows:

Vaccination Situation After 8:00 AM yesterday, the Municipal Health Bureau sent doctors and nurses to the cholera prevention vaccination station at the North Railway Station. All travelers and pedestrians were advised to get vaccinated until 12:00 PM. In the afternoon, doctors and nurses from the Health Department of the Two-Road Administration Bureau continued to advise travelers and civilians to get vaccinated until 6:00 PM. Another team of doctors and nurses went to the municipal elementary schools in the North and South City early yesterday morning (the names of the schools were listed in yesterday's newspaper) to administer vaccinations. In the afternoon, key members of the bureau's prevention section, accompanied by six doctors and nurses and more than ten sanitary police officers, first stationed themselves near the Guanqiao Bridge in the South City. The officers held up the large yellow umbrellas they were carrying, and four small tables were set up under the umbrellas, displaying various medical instruments. In a short while, citizens came to watch the umbrellas in an endless stream. The doctors and nurses immediately went forward to explain the dangers of cholera to the citizens, stating that getting vaccinated could avoid the risk of infection. The doctors then instructed the onlookers to get vaccinated one by one. After about an hour, three or four hundred people had been vaccinated. They then went to the bridge pier on Hengfeng Road to advise pedestrians to get vaccinated, it is said.

Slogans Everywhere The bureau has been posting wall slogans in the city's major transportation hubs for several days. As of yesterday afternoon, the bureau still sent staff to the north and south transportation routes to inspect and paste wall slogans, which were mostly completed. Health slogans on the walls of various tram stops and thoroughfares were visible everywhere. Yesterday, slogans were also found on various trams, buses, and long-distance buses of the China Merchants Tram Company. In order to achieve widespread coverage, the bureau will order staff to inspect and add more slogans on various vehicles starting tomorrow. The number of slogans on rickshaws increased yesterday.

Vaccination Suspension Today The bureau has decided to suspend vaccination for one day today, as it is Sunday. Staff members and doctors in various departments have been very busy preparing for publicity and implementation in recent days, and need to rest.

Chen Mingshu Departed from Shanghai Only Yesterday

Taking the Ryota Maru to Japan

After arriving in Shanghai, Chen Mingshu, Chairman of the Guangdong Provincial Government, kept his whereabouts very secret. This newspaper previously reported, based on the words of his Secretary-General Sun Xiwwen to reporters from various newspapers, that Chen had left for Japan on the morning of the 13th aboard the British mail ship Cachemaille. On the same day, various newspapers also carried similar reports. According to reliable sources, Chen had not left Shanghai at that time because he still needed to contact the central government about the Guangdong affairs. After Chen met with Liu Wendao, a representative of the central government, the issue came to a conclusion. Liu returned to Nanjing the night before yesterday, and Chen Mingshu, accompanied by Secretary Yang Jianping and one staff member, left Shanghai for Japan at 8:00 AM yesterday aboard the Japanese mail ship Ryota Maru. His ticket was purchased to Kobe, and from Kobe, he would take a train to Tokyo. He is scheduled to stay for more than a month before deciding on his next move.

The Buddhist Association Presents Memoranda on Tibetan Affairs

Document Presented to the National Government

Regarding the discord between the Dalai Lama and the Panchen Lama in Tibet, the Chinese Buddhist Association presented a document to the National Government, requesting the selection and dispatch of Han and Mongolian Buddhist leaders to Tibet to explain that the Dalai Lama welcomes the Panchen Lama to return to Tibet, so as to strengthen the border and prevent foreign covetousness. The document states, "Tibet has a vast territory and is adjacent to British India. It is rich in resources and has long been eyed by the British. This time, the Dalai Lama and the Panchen Lama are at odds, and the Panchen Lama has left. The Dalai Lama is also repeatedly waging war on the Sichuan border. It is difficult to guarantee that he has not been fooled by foreigners. Tibet is our country's territory, and if we let him do as he pleases, it is feared that the imperialists will wantonly invade, and the western border will be breached. Taixu and others are deeply worried about this. Yesterday, Taixu specially visited the Panchen Lama and his entourage, advising him to cease strife with the Dalai Lama, which was greatly appreciated. However, the Dalai Lama's side has not yet agreed. It is proposed to ask the Chairman to follow his belief in Buddhism and quickly select and dispatch one Han and one Mongolian Buddhist leader, setting a deadline for them to enter Tibet. Using the great meaning of Buddhism's selfless non-contention, they should explain to the Dalai Lama and his entourage, and make them understand the profound interests. They should make them convinced so that the Dalai Lama and the Panchen Lama will first automatically send a joint telegram, releasing suspicion and returning to harmony. Then, the Dalai Lama and his entourage will welcome the Panchen Lama and his entourage back to Tibet, so that the Dalai Lama and the Panchen Lama can be in their respective positions, strengthening the Tibetan people's inward orientation, thereby strengthening the border and preventing foreign covetousness. Is this appropriate? We hereby present this with respect, and respectfully request your approval and implementation. It is truly both public and virtuous," and so on.

Bids for the New Municipal Government Building Opened Yesterday

Winner: Zhu Senji Construction Company

Bid Price: 548,000 Yuan

Since the bidding for the new municipal government building to be built in the city center area was announced, the bidders have been very enthusiastic, all of whom are well-known construction companies in Shanghai. Yesterday at 2:00 PM was the day for opening bids. The location was in the auditorium of the Municipal Public Works Bureau. The municipal government specially sent Cai Zengji, Director of the Municipal Finance Bureau, to supervise the event. Attendees from the Public Works Bureau included Director Shen Yi and the chiefs and technical officers of various departments. The City Center Area Construction Committee sent representatives Xu Peihuang, Xi Dingmo, and Zhu Yan to participate in the bid opening. Military Law Tribunal Established on the 19th

Presiding Judge and Judges

Take Oath of Office on the Same Day

Regarding the preparations by the Songhu Garrison Command, together with the Shanghai Municipal Government, the Shanghai Special City Party Department, and the Jiangsu Higher Court, to organize a Shanghai Municipal Provisional Military Law Tribunal, as previously reported, it is now learned that the tribunal has been organized and is ready. Each participating institution has appointed judges, including Jiang Huaisu, Huang Daolin, Qian Chengjun, Chen Hanzuo, and Dai Yuanchuan, all of whom have arrived. A meeting was held on the 15th, and Chen Hanzuo was publicly elected as the presiding judge. The tribunal is scheduled to be established and begin operations on the morning of the 19th of this month at 10:00 AM. The presiding judge and all judges are also scheduled to take the oath of office on that day. The address of the tribunal is located within the Songhu Garrison Command, at the former site of the Political Training Department of the Garrison Command. In addition to the judges, the internal organization consists of only one chief clerk, four clerks, and three recorders, all of whom are said to be concurrently serving personnel appointed by the participating institutions.

All Circles Support the People's Convention's Declaration on Abolishing Treaties

Third District Party Department The Third District Party Department issued a declaration, the gist of which is as follows: (Omitted titles) Our country has been bound by unequal treaties for eighty years, leading to the bankruptcy of industry and the weakness of national strength. Thinking of this, we feel deeply pained. Now, the National Convention, based on the teachings of the Premier and in accordance with the demands of the people, has resolutely and voluntarily declared their abolition. All Chinese people are celebrating this in unison. However, at the beginning of this treaty abolition, all compatriots across the country should be diligent, persevering, courageous, and progressive, so that the happiness of freedom and equality may shine without bounds. On the government's side, efforts should be made to improve domestic politics and promote proposed projects. Those engaged in agriculture, industry, and commerce should strive to improve production technology and enrich the national economy. Those involved in education should study practical sciences to avoid borrowing talent from foreign countries. Only then can the realization of the Three Principles of the People and the era of global harmony be within reach. This declaration is hereby made, hoping to be remembered. The Executive Committee of the Third District of the Shanghai Special City of the Kuomintang.

National Products Maintenance Association The China National Products Maintenance Association telegraphed the National Convention yesterday, stating, "To the esteemed representatives of the National Convention in the capital: Our country has been bound by unequal treaties for decades, hindering our development, undermining our construction, and even leading to the invasion of our territory and the usurpation of our national rights. Laws, customs duties, and everything else have been trampled upon. As a result, the national economy and the people's livelihood have suffered greatly. Internal strife has arisen repeatedly, and the country is on the verge of ruin. If we do not take practical measures to cure this, how can we survive? We have found that our friendly nations are not lacking in enlightened individuals and countries upholding justice, and they have already abolished these treaties one after another. Only a few countries remain, still insatiable in their ambitions, intending to delay and preserve their tools of aggression. Fortunately, your convention, adhering to the last wishes of the late Premier, has issued a declaration voluntarily abolishing unequal treaties and proclaiming this to the world. The words are righteous and the arguments are sound. Our association, as a group representing the entire national products industry, has long suffered from the pain of unequal treaties and has been deeply harmed. Therefore, we especially support the declaration of abolition and vow to support it with the utmost sincerity, striving for its thorough realization, regardless of any difficulties or sacrifices. We hereby telegraph our support, hoping you will take it into consideration." Standing Committee Members of the China National Products Maintenance Association, Wang Jiean, Wang Xingyi, and Wang Hanqiang, respectfully bow.

Supporting the Declaration on the Voluntary Abolition of Unequal Treaties

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China received telegrams yesterday from the Federations of Chambers of Commerce of Henan and Hunan provinces. Details are listed below:

Please Voluntarily Abolish Consular Jurisdiction "Our country has been bound by unequal treaties for decades, and the consular jurisdiction is the most painful for our business community. Whenever there are commercial lawsuits involving Chinese and foreigners, foreign consuls invariably favor their own merchants. Even if we win the lawsuit, there are many difficulties in execution, and there are rarely satisfactory results. The late Premier taught that the abolition of unequal treaties was of utmost importance, and the current government also has plans to reclaim legal rights. However, since foreigners rely on this as a tool of aggression, they will inevitably obstruct it in various ways to pursue their own interests. We implore the central government to resolutely take action and immediately announce the abolition of consular jurisdiction to maintain the judicial system and the sovereignty of the entire territory. This office, on behalf of the entire business community of the province, stands as your support. We send this telegram with indignation, hoping you will take it into consideration." Prepared by the Preparatory Office of the Federation of Chambers of Commerce of Hunan Province.

Please Resolutely Abolish Unequal Treaties "(Titles Omitted) Since the Manchus entered and ruled our country, public opinion has completely disappeared, and sovereignty has been controlled by the monarch, who rashly represented the entire people with his personal will. Since the Opium War in 1840, the true image of corruption has been completely exposed, leading to imperialists with aggressive policies swarming in. Taking advantage of our nation's lack of awareness, they used cannons and warships to intimidate the weak and incompetent Qing government, forcing it to sign various unequal treaties that did not represent the will of the people, placing the entire country in a semi-colonial position for ninety years. It was the ultimate humiliation of losing national rights and sovereignty. Our late Premier, worried about the government's ignorance and hating the bullying of various countries, initiated the revolution, overthrew the Qing Dynasty, and revealed the true meaning of national self-determination as a warning to prevent the aggression of the great powers. Therefore, the early years of the Republic had a completely new outlook. Unfortunately, the nation's fortunes declined, and warlords rose up one after another, fabricating falsehoods and slandering without restraint, violating public opinion and losing rights and interests, and flattering the great powers to consolidate their political power. The decline of our international status became even more irreversible. Under these critical circumstances, we must strive to fight for the liberation of our nation, and we must automatically abolish unequal treaties that do not represent the will of the people to consolidate our national foundation. Moreover, imperialists have always regarded the subjugation of weak nations as their duty, and wherever there is profit, they flock to it like ducks. To expect them to abolish the old treaties is like seeking skins from a tiger. Even in the current negotiations for the abolition of consular jurisdiction, our government has long declared its intention to abolish it on a set date, but the various imperialists are ambivalent, delaying and procrastinating, and their intentions are to use cunning means to seek a final reservation. National sovereignty resides in the people, and unequal treaties concluded in violation of public opinion are not only absolutely unacceptable to our citizens, but also fundamentally cannot have legal effect. Yet, imperialists disregard human rights, ignore justice, and do not hesitate to use base means to seek their own interests, infringing upon our sovereignty and suppressing our public opinion. If we continue to delay and make mistakes, and do not resolutely abolish these treaties, the future of our country will be truly unimaginable. We hope that our people will awaken deeply, strive to invigorate themselves, unite the will of the people, and, with a spirit of great fearlessness, deal with the imperialists, act as a support for the central government, and not stop until the goal of abolition is achieved. On this day when the National Convention begins, we announce the abolition of unequal treaties. The late Premier's words are still ringing in our ears. We wish our people to quickly plan for this together. We send this urgent telegram, with the utmost anticipation." Sent by the Kaifeng Chamber of Commerce in Henan Province.

The Consolidated Tax Bureau Abolishes Resident Postal Offices

Replaced by Customs Resident Postal Offices for Collection

The Ministry of Finance had previously ordered the Consolidated Tax Bureau of this port to abolish all Customs offices nationwide. This measure was implemented yesterday. The Ministry of Finance also stated that since the Shanghai Postal Administration also has offices set up by the Consolidated Tax Bureau, and their nature is the same as that of the resident Customs offices, they should also be abolished in a uniform manner. Therefore, the Consolidated Tax Bureau was ordered to comply uniformly some days ago. The Consolidated Tax Bureau, after receiving the order, also abolished them yesterday. All procedures for collecting consolidated taxes at post offices have been transferred to the Customs resident postal offices.

Draft Special Trade Union Law

National Convention Submits to the National Government for Reference

The Draft Special Trade Union Law, drafted by the Postal Workers' Union and submitted by more than one hundred representatives of the labor circle, including Hou Dachun, to the National Convention, has been learned to have been submitted by the Presidium of the Convention on the 13th to the Proposal Review Committee for review. The Committee deemed that it had sufficient reasons. However, due to the large number of proposals before the Convention, except for a small number of important proposals concerning the entire situation, which should be submitted to the Convention for discussion, most of the other proposals involved individual scopes or had already established principles and only required expediting, and it was not necessary to present them for discussion one by one during the Convention's brief period. The Special Trade Union Law and the Trade Union Law are to be implemented in parallel, and their promulgation should not be a problem. The 54 articles of the draft proposed by the Postal Workers' Union have pure aims and advocate for mixed employee organizations, breaking down the bad phenomenon of separation between superiors and subordinates. It proposes a general organization so that national actions can all be brought onto the right track. Overall, it is generally applicable. Therefore, the Proposal Review Committee has submitted the draft, etc., to the National Government for reference when formally enacting the law. Such an expedient arrangement, taking into account all parties, is greatly admired for the spirit of the Convention. It is expected that after the National Convention closes, the future of the labor movement will have new developments.

Appeal to Ban the Cutting of Paulownia and Pine Trees in Zhejiang Province

The National Products Factory Association Telegraphed the Ministry of Industry

The Shanghai National Products Factory Federation telegraphed the Ministry of Industry yesterday, stating, "Member Heji Umbrella Hook Factory, for the convenience of procuring raw materials, has set up a branch in the Jin Clan Ancestral Hall north of Ninghai County, Zhejiang Province, where Zheng Jijian and Dai Minggao purchase paulownia and pine trees from various places to manufacture umbrella hooks to resist imported goods. These raw materials are collected sporadically from nearby villagers on the mountains and are small paulownia and pine trees that have been growing for years, usually only used as firewood. The factory values their ease of bending, so they paint them with black lacquer to use as umbrella handles, turning useless materials into useful ones. In terms of promoting industry, it is necessary to maintain this small craft. However, the local Public Security Bureau, listening to biased opinions, claimed that it was harming the forest and prohibited procurement and sent police to order a shutdown, a measure that is particularly inappropriate. Therefore, we hereby telegraph and request your ministry to consider that the factory was established to resist foreign goods, and dozens of workers rely on it for a living. Once it is closed, it not only goes against the intention of promoting national products, but also causes dozens of workers to lose their jobs. We urge you to transfer this to the Zhejiang Provincial Government and instruct the county government to quickly lift the ban."

May 20th

When the school buildings were closed by force, the students suddenly lost their home. They had no choice but to send representatives to the capital to appeal to the Ministry of Education. Those in society who sympathized with our school also actively urged the government to maintain the school.
